\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Main interface class of the Agora Native S\+DK.

Call the methods of this class to use all the functionalities of the S\+DK. Agora recommends calling the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} A\+PI methods in the same thread instead of in multiple threads. In previous versions, this class was named Agora\+Audio, and was renamed to \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} from version 1.\+0. 

\doxysubsection{Member Function Documentation}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a30d9a5c1a0e0500e8f5b94c2063450d5}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a30d9a5c1a0e0500e8f5b94c2063450d5}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!create@{create}}
\index{create@{create}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{create()}{create()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static synchronized \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+create (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Context}]{context,  }\item[{String}]{app\+Id,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler}{I\+Rtc\+Engine\+Event\+Handler}}}]{handler }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) throws Exception\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Creates an \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} instance.

Unless otherwise specified, all the methods provided by the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} class are executed asynchronously. Agora recommends calling these methods in the same thread.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item You must create an \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} instance before calling any other method.
\item You can create an \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} instance either by calling this method or by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_afffd4c0d9b799631ed407c5167b6e09a}{create2}}. The difference between \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_afffd4c0d9b799631ed407c5167b6e09a}{create2}} and this method is that \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_afffd4c0d9b799631ed407c5167b6e09a}{create2}} enables you to specify the connection area.
\item The Agora R\+TC Native S\+DK supports creating only one \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} instance for an app for now.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em context} & The context of Android Activity. \\
\hline
{\em app\+Id} & The App ID issued to you by Agora. See \href{https://docs.agora.io/en/Agora\%20Platform/token\#get-an-app-id}{\texttt{ How to get the App ID}}. Only users in apps with the same App ID can join the same channel and communicate with each other. Use an App ID to create only one \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} instance. To change your App ID, call destroy to \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a87e95e4a63d9f2ff9f04f632ffccfce8}{destroy}} the current \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} instance and then call {\ttfamily create} to create an \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} instance with the new App ID. \\
\hline
{\em handler} & \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler}{I\+Rtc\+Engine\+Event\+Handler}} is an abstract class providing default implementation. The S\+DK uses this class to report to the app on S\+DK runtime events. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} instance, if the method call succeeds.
\item $<$ 0, if the method call fails. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em Exception} & Fails to create an \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} instance. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_afffd4c0d9b799631ed407c5167b6e09a}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_afffd4c0d9b799631ed407c5167b6e09a}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!create@{create}}
\index{create@{create}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{create()}{create()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static synchronized \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+create (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_config}{Rtc\+Engine\+Config}}}]{config }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) throws Exception\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Creates an \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} instance.

The Agora Native S\+DK only supports one \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} instance at a time, therefore the app should create one \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} object only. Unless otherwise specified\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item All called methods provided by the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} class are executed asynchronously. We recommends calling these methods in the same thread.
\item The following rule applies to all A\+P\+Is whose return values are integer types\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: The method call succeeds.
\item $<$ 0\+: The method call fails.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Ensure that you call this method before calling any other A\+PI.
\item Only users with the same App ID can join the same channel and call each other.
\item An App ID can create only one \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} object. For multiple App I\+Ds in an app, you need to create multiple \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} objects. Call \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a87e95e4a63d9f2ff9f04f632ffccfce8}{destroy}} first to destroy the current \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} instance before calling this method.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em config} & Configurations for the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} instance. For details, see \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_config}{\}.  An Rtc\+Engine object.  Exception Fails to create an Rtc\+Engine instance. }}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a87e95e4a63d9f2ff9f04f632ffccfce8}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a87e95e4a63d9f2ff9f04f632ffccfce8}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!destroy@{destroy}}
\index{destroy@{destroy}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{destroy()}{destroy()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static synchronized void io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+destroy (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Releases all the resources used by the Agora S\+DK.

This method is useful for apps that occasionally make voice or video calls, to free up resources for other operations when not making calls.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Do not immediately uninstall the S\+DK\textquotesingle{}s dynamic library after the call, or it may crash because the S\+DK clean-\/up thread has not quit.
\item Call this method in the sub-\/thread.
\item Once the app destroys the created \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} instance, you cannot use any method or callback in the S\+DK. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_aa6eb91768f2a6efedb6f581e9a42bed0}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_aa6eb91768f2a6efedb6f581e9a42bed0}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!setChannelProfile@{setChannelProfile}}
\index{setChannelProfile@{setChannelProfile}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setChannelProfile()}{setChannelProfile()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Channel\+Profile (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{profile }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets the channel profile.

The \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} differentiates channel profiles and applies different optimization algorithms accordingly. For example, it prioritizes smoothness and low latency for a video call, and prioritizes video quality for a video broadcast.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item To ensure the quality of real-\/time communication, we recommend that all users in a channel use the same channel profile.
\item Call this method before calling {\ttfamily join\+Channel}. You cannot set the channel profile once you have joined the channel.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em profile} & The channel profile\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily C\+H\+A\+N\+N\+E\+L\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+M\+M\+U\+N\+I\+C\+A\+T\+I\+ON}(0)\+: Communication. Use this profile when there are two users in the channel.
\item {\ttfamily C\+H\+A\+N\+N\+E\+L\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+L\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+I\+NG}(1)\+: (Default) Live Broadcast. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a079013f8c575a75834e2787ee869413e}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a079013f8c575a75834e2787ee869413e}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!setClientRole@{setClientRole}}
\index{setClientRole@{setClientRole}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setClientRole()}{setClientRole()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Client\+Role (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{role }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets the role of a user.

This method sets the user role as either B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+ER or A\+U\+D\+I\+E\+N\+CE (default).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The broadcaster sends and receives streams.
\item The audience receives streams only.
\end{DoxyItemize}

By default, all users are audience regardless of the channel profile. Call this method to change the user role to B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+ER so that the user can send a stream.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
After calling the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a079013f8c575a75834e2787ee869413e}{set\+Client\+Role()}} method to C\+L\+I\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+O\+L\+E\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+E\+N\+CE, the S\+DK stops audio recording. However, C\+L\+I\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+O\+L\+E\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+E\+N\+CE will keep audio recording with A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+S\+C\+E\+N\+A\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+C\+H\+A\+T\+R\+O\+O\+M(5). Normally, app developer can also use mute api to achieve the same result, and we implement this \textquotesingle{}non-\/orthogonal\textquotesingle{} behavior only to make A\+PI backward compatible.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em role} & The role of the client\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily C\+L\+I\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+O\+L\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+ER}(1)\+: The broadcaster.
\item {\ttfamily C\+L\+I\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+O\+L\+E\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+E\+N\+C\+E(2)}\+: The audience. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_ae61dcff88a6c9854770fbd8cf14310f3}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_ae61dcff88a6c9854770fbd8cf14310f3}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!setClientRole@{setClientRole}}
\index{setClientRole@{setClientRole}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setClientRole()}{setClientRole()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Client\+Role (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{role,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_client_role_options}{Client\+Role\+Options}}}]{options }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets the role of a user ({\ttfamily L\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+I\+NG} profile only).

This method sets the role of a user, such as a host or an audience (default), before joining a channel.

This method can be used to switch the user role after a user joins a channel. In the {\ttfamily L\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+I\+NG} profile, when a user switches user roles after joining a channel, a successful set\+Client\+Role method call triggers the following callbacks\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The local client\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_aea843919d9cb5c5dab0ed175fdd92959}{on\+Client\+Role\+Changed}}.
\item The remote client\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a848d29acef97523964bb27dd5b637162}{on\+User\+Joined}} or \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a36dfe32e633612d8e74e1a32c504c817}{on\+User\+Offline\}(U\+S\+E\+R\+\_\+\+O\+F\+F\+L\+I\+N\+E\+\_\+\+B\+E\+C\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+E\+N\+CE).  role Sets the role of a user\+:{\ttfamily C\+L\+I\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+O\+L\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+ER}(1)\+: Host. A host can both send and receive streams.{\ttfamily C\+L\+I\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+O\+L\+E\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+E\+N\+CE}(2)\+: Audience, the default role. An audience can only receive streams.  options Client role options of a user, see \#\+Client\+Role\+Options. 0(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+OK)\+: Success.$<$ 0\+: Failure.-\/1(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED)\+: A general error occurs (no specified reason).-\/2(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+R\+G\+U\+M\+E\+NT)\+: The parameter is invalid.-\/7(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+I\+N\+I\+T\+I\+A\+L\+I\+Z\+ED)\+: The S\+DK is not initialized. }}
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a53300ddeb64455cd7f7d7c2eb3f08d1e}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a53300ddeb64455cd7f7d7c2eb3f08d1e}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!sendCustomReportMessage@{sendCustomReportMessage}}
\index{sendCustomReportMessage@{sendCustomReportMessage}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{sendCustomReportMessage()}{sendCustomReportMessage()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+send\+Custom\+Report\+Message (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{id,  }\item[{String}]{category,  }\item[{String}]{event,  }\item[{String}]{label,  }\item[{int}]{value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Agora supports reporting and analyzing customized messages.

This function is in the beta stage with a free trial. The ability provided in its beta test version is reporting a maximum of 10 message pieces within 6 seconds, with each message piece not exceeding 256 bytes.

To try out this function, contact \href{mailto:support@agora.io}{\texttt{ support@agora.\+io}} and discuss the format of customized messages with us. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a9f46b1374bf38be28d65682b0ea6ade9}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a9f46b1374bf38be28d65682b0ea6ade9}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!joinChannel@{joinChannel}}
\index{joinChannel@{joinChannel}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{joinChannel()}{joinChannel()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+join\+Channel (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{token,  }\item[{String}]{channel\+Name,  }\item[{String}]{optional\+Info,  }\item[{int}]{optional\+Uid }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Joins a channel.

Users in the same channel can talk to each other; and multiple users in the same channel can start a group chat. Note that users using different App I\+Ds cannot call each other.

Once in a call, the user must call the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_af3fe5d61a9ca8db36b56432273d02307}{leave\+Channel}} method to exit the current call before entering another channel.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This method allows you to join only one channel at a time.
\item A channel does not accept duplicate {\ttfamily uid}s, that is, two users with the same uid. If you set {\ttfamily uid} as 0, the system automatically assigns a user ID.
\item Ensure that the app ID you use to generate the token is the same app ID that you pass in the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a30d9a5c1a0e0500e8f5b94c2063450d5}{create}} method.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em token} & The token for authentication.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item In situations not requiring high security\+: You can use the temporary token generated at Console. For details, see \href{https://docs.agora.io/en/Agora\%20Platform/token?platform=All\%20Platforms\#get-a-temporary-token}{\texttt{ Get a temporary token}}.
\item In situations requiring high security\+: Set it as the token generated at you server. For details, see \href{https://docs.agora.io/en/Agora\%20Platform/token?platform=All\%20Platforms\#get-a-token}{\texttt{ Generate a token}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em channel\+Name} & The unique channel name for the Agora\+R\+TC session in the string format. The string length must be less than 64 bytes. Supported character scopes are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item All lowercase English letters\+: a to z.
\item All uppercase English letters\+: A to Z.
\item All numeric characters\+: 0 to 9.
\item The space character.
\item Punctuation characters and other symbols, including\+: \char`\"{}!\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\#\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\%\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\&\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}(\char`\"{}, \char`\"{})\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}+\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}-\/\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+:\char`\"{}, \char`\"{};\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$<$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}=\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}.\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$>$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}?\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}@\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\mbox{[}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\mbox{]}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$^\wedge$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+\_\+\char`\"{}, \char`\"{} \{\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$\vert$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$\sim$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{},\char`\"{}. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em optional\+Info} & (Optional) Additional information about the channel that you want to add. It can be set as a N\+U\+LL string or channel related information. Other users in the channel will not receive this message. \\
\hline
{\em optional\+Uid} & (Optional) User ID\+: A 32-\/bit unsigned integer ranging from 1 to (2$^\wedge$32-\/1). It must be unique. If not assigned (or set to 0), the S\+DK assigns one and reports it in the \mbox{\hyperlink{}{on\+Join\+Channel\+Success}} callback. Your app must record and maintain the returned value as the S\+DK does not maintain it.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_aed8279d06ee29f1cd6c4ca029cb63514}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_aed8279d06ee29f1cd6c4ca029cb63514}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!joinChannel@{joinChannel}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{joinChannel()}{joinChannel()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+join\+Channel (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{token,  }\item[{String}]{channel\+Id,  }\item[{int}]{uid,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_channel_media_options}{Channel\+Media\+Options}}}]{options }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Joins a channel with media options.

Users in the same channel can talk to each other; and multiple users in the same channel can start a group chat. Note that users using different App I\+Ds cannot call each other.

Once in a call, the user must call the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_af3fe5d61a9ca8db36b56432273d02307}{leave\+Channel}} method to exit the current call before entering another channel.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This method allows you to join only one channel at a time.
\item A channel does not accept duplicate {\ttfamily uid}s, that is, two users with the same uid. If you set {\ttfamily uid} as 0, the system automatically assigns a user ID.
\item Ensure that the app ID you use to generate the token is the same app ID that you pass in the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a30d9a5c1a0e0500e8f5b94c2063450d5}{create}} method.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\item In situations requiring high security\+: Set it as the token generated at you server. For details, see \href{https://docs.agora.io/en/Agora\%20Platform/token?platform=All\%20Platforms\#get-a-token}{\texttt{ Generate a token}}.

Your app must record and maintain the returned value as the S\+DK does not maintain it. \\

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_af3fe5d61a9ca8db36b56432273d02307}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_af3fe5d61a9ca8db36b56432273d02307}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!leaveChannel@{leaveChannel}}
\index{leaveChannel@{leaveChannel}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{leaveChannel()}{leaveChannel()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+leave\+Channel (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Leaves the channel.

This method allows a user to leave the channel, for example, by hanging up or exiting a call.

After joining a channel, the user must call this method to end the current call before joining another one. This method also releases all resources related to the call.

This method is an asynchronous call, which means that the result of this method returns even before the user has not actually left the channel. Once the user successfully leaves the channel, the S\+DK triggers the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler}{on\+Leave\+Channel}} callback.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If you call \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a87e95e4a63d9f2ff9f04f632ffccfce8}{destroy}} immediately after this method, the leave\+Channel process will be interrupted, and the S\+DK will not trigger the {\ttfamily on\+Leave\+Channel} callback.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_ab4af0c1df4b68eb898b1843dd0671702}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_ab4af0c1df4b68eb898b1843dd0671702}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!leaveChannel@{leaveChannel}}
\index{leaveChannel@{leaveChannel}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}

Once the user successfully leaves the channel, the S\+DK triggers the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_ae8d95d70238163de3d89399bee8061a1}{on\+Leave\+Channel}} callback.

\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!renewToken@{renewToken}}
\index{renewToken@{renewToken}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{renewToken()}{renewToken()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+renew\+Token (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{token }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Renews the token.

Once a token is enabled and used, it expires after a certain period of time.

Under the following circumstances, generate a new token on your server, and then call this method to renew it. Failure to do so results in the S\+DK disconnecting from the server.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_ad230797ab45c4307562e1b19519253b5}{on\+Token\+Privilege\+Will\+Expire}} callback is triggered;
\item The \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a2585f098b637d03ae3aca03daaca8eef}{on\+Request\+Token}} callback is triggered;
\item The {\ttfamily E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+T\+O\+K\+E\+N\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+I\+R\+ED(-\/109)} error is reported.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em token} & The new token. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a9d596bab97c3b7b164e9f7a61732da4b}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a9d596bab97c3b7b164e9f7a61732da4b}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!registerLocalUserAccount@{registerLocalUserAccount}}
\index{registerLocalUserAccount@{registerLocalUserAccount}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{registerLocalUserAccount()}{registerLocalUserAccount()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+register\+Local\+User\+Account (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{app\+Id,  }\item[{String}]{user\+Account }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Registers a user account.

Once registered, the user account can be used to identify the local user when the user joins the channel. After the user successfully registers a user account, the S\+DK triggers the on\+Local\+User\+Registered callback on the local client, reporting the user ID and user account of the local user.

To join a channel with a user account, you can choose either of the following\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Call the register\+Local\+User\+Account method to create a user account, and then the join\+Channel\+With\+User\+Account method to join the channel.
\item Call the join\+Channel\+With\+User\+Account method to join the channel.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The difference between the two is that for the former, the time elapsed between calling the join\+Channel\+With\+User\+Account method and joining the channel is shorter than the latter.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Ensure that you set the {\ttfamily user\+Account} parameter. Otherwise, this method does not take effect.
\item Ensure that the value of the {\ttfamily user\+Account} parameter is unique in the channel.
\item To ensure smooth communication, use the same parameter type to identify the user. For example, if a user joins the channel with a user ID, then ensure all the other users use the user ID too. The same applies to the user account. If a user joins the channel with the Agora Web S\+DK, ensure that the uid of the user is set to the same parameter type.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em app\+Id} & The App ID of your project. \\
\hline
{\em user\+Account} & The user account. The maximum length of this parameter is 255 bytes. Ensure that you set this parameter and do not set it as null. Supported character scopes are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item All lowercase English letters\+: a to z.
\item All uppercase English letters\+: A to Z.
\item All numeric characters\+: 0 to 9.
\item The space character.
\item Punctuation characters and other symbols, including\+: \char`\"{}!\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\#\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\%\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\&\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}(\char`\"{}, \char`\"{})\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}+\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}-\/\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+:\char`\"{}, \char`\"{};\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$<$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}=\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}.\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$>$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}?\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}@\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\mbox{[}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\mbox{]}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$^\wedge$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+\_\+\char`\"{}, \char`\"{} \{\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$\vert$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$\sim$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{},\char`\"{}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline

\begin{DoxyItemize}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_aef5f666b23319116e7d7ee85e58fc5e8}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_aef5f666b23319116e7d7ee85e58fc5e8}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!joinChannelWithUserAccount@{joinChannelWithUserAccount}}
\index{joinChannelWithUserAccount@{joinChannelWithUserAccount}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{joinChannelWithUserAccount()}{joinChannelWithUserAccount()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+join\+Channel\+With\+User\+Account (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{token,  }\item[{String}]{channel\+Name,  }\item[{String}]{user\+Account }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Joins the channel with a user account.

After the user successfully joins the channel, the S\+DK triggers the following callbacks\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The local client\+: on\+Local\+User\+Registered and on\+Join\+Channel\+Success . The remote client\+: on\+User\+Joined and on\+User\+Info\+Updated , if the user joining the channel is in the {\ttfamily C\+O\+M\+M\+U\+N\+I\+C\+A\+T\+I\+ON} profile, or is a host in the {\ttfamily L\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+I\+NG} profile.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
To ensure smooth communication, use the same parameter type to identify the user. For example, if a user joins the channel with a user ID, then ensure all the other users use the user ID too. The same applies to the user account. If a user joins the channel with the Agora Web S\+DK, ensure that the uid of the user is set to the same parameter type.
\end{DoxyNote}

\item For high-\/security requirements\+: Set it as the token generated at your server. For details, see \href{https://docs.agora.io/en/Voice/token?platform=All\%20Platforms\#get-a-token}{\texttt{ Get a token}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a65d0e8211e6a9ac4dde5d67ced844cfa}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a65d0e8211e6a9ac4dde5d67ced844cfa}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!joinChannelWithUserAccount@{joinChannelWithUserAccount}}
\index{joinChannelWithUserAccount@{joinChannelWithUserAccount}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{joinChannelWithUserAccount()}{joinChannelWithUserAccount()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+join\+Channel\+With\+User\+Account (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{token,  }\item[{String}]{channel\+Name,  }\item[{String}]{user\+Account,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_channel_media_options}{Channel\+Media\+Options}}}]{options }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Joins the channel with a user account, and configures whether to automatically subscribe to audio or video streams after joining the channel. \begin{DoxySince}{Since}
v3.\+3.\+0.
\end{DoxySince}
After the user successfully joins the channel, the S\+DK triggers the following callbacks\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The local client\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a8643b8a54c5aa30e22209a54274fbcf3}{on\+Local\+User\+Registered}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a25a599788cbb7d9b97b9f67747c17243}{on\+Join\+Channel\+Success}}.
\item The remote client\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a848d29acef97523964bb27dd5b637162}{on\+User\+Joined}} and \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a0cd49bb3b8733f04ecaacf1df091e07f}{on\+User\+Info\+Updated\}, if the user joining the channel is in the {\ttfamily C\+O\+M\+M\+U\+N\+I\+C\+A\+T\+I\+ON} profile, or is a host in the {\ttfamily L\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+I\+NG} profile. Compared with  Rtc\+Engine\#join\+Channel\+With\+User\+Account(String token, String channel\+Name, String user\+Account) join\+Channel\+With\+User\+Account\}\mbox{[}1/2\mbox{]}, this method has the {\ttfamily options} parameter to configure whether the end user automatically subscribes to all remote audio and video streams in a channel when joining the channel. By default, the user subscribes to the audio and video streams of all the other users in the channel, thus incurring all associated usage costs. To unsubscribe, set the {\ttfamily options} parameter or call the {\ttfamily mute} methods accordingly.To ensure smooth communication, use the same parameter type to identify the user. For example, if a user joins the channel with a user ID, then ensure all the other users use the user ID too. The same applies to the user account. If a user joins the channel with the Agora Web S\+DK, ensure that the uid of the user is set to the same parameter type.  token The token generated at your server. For details, see }}Generate a token. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em channel\+Name} & The channel name. The maximum length of this parameter is 64 bytes. Supported character scopes are\+:\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\item All lowercase English letters\+: a to z.
\item All uppercase English letters\+: A to Z.
\item All numeric characters\+: 0 to 9.
\item The space character.
\item Punctuation characters and other symbols, including\+: \char`\"{}!\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\#\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\%\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\&\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}(\char`\"{}, \char`\"{})\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}+\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}-\/\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+:\char`\"{}, \char`\"{};\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$<$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}=\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}.\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$>$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}?\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}@\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\mbox{[}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\mbox{]}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$^\wedge$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+\_\+\char`\"{}, \char`\"{} \{\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$\vert$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$\sim$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{},\char`\"{}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em user\+Account} & The user account. The maximum length of this parameter is 255 bytes. Ensure that you set this parameter and do not set it as null.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\item All lowercase English letters\+: a to z.
\item All uppercase English letters\+: A to Z.
\item All numeric characters\+: 0 to 9.
\item The space character.
\item Punctuation characters and other symbols, including\+: \char`\"{}!\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\#\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\%\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\&\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}(\char`\"{}, \char`\"{})\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}+\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}-\/\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+:\char`\"{}, \char`\"{};\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$<$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}=\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}.\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$>$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}?\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}@\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\mbox{[}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\mbox{]}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$^\wedge$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+\_\+\char`\"{}, \char`\"{} \{\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$\vert$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$\sim$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{},\char`\"{}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getUserInfoByUserAccount()}{getUserInfoByUserAccount()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+get\+User\+Info\+By\+User\+Account (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{user\+Account,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_user_info}{User\+Info}}}]{user\+Info }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Gets the user information by passing in the user account.

After a remote user joins the channel, the S\+DK gets the user ID and user account of the remote user, caches them in a mapping table object ({\ttfamily user\+Info}), and triggers the on\+User\+Info\+Updated callback on the local client.

After receiving the oon\+User\+Info\+Updated callback, you can call this method to get the user ID of the remote user from the {\ttfamily user\+Info} object by passing in the user account.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em user\+Account} & The user account of the user. Ensure that you set this parameter. \\
\hline
{\em user\+Info} & A user\+Info object that identifies the user\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\item To set the audio scenario, call \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_afffd4c0d9b799631ed407c5167b6e09a}{create2}} and pass value in the {\ttfamily m\+Audio\+Scenario} member.

\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!setHighQualityAudioParameters@{setHighQualityAudioParameters}}
\index{setHighQualityAudioParameters@{setHighQualityAudioParameters}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setHighQualityAudioParameters()}{setHighQualityAudioParameters()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+High\+Quality\+Audio\+Parameters (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{boolean}]{fullband,  }\item[{boolean}]{stereo,  }\item[{boolean}]{full\+Bitrate }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets high-\/quality audio preferences.

Call this method and set all the modes before joining a channel. Do N\+OT call this method again after joining a channel.

Note\+: Agora does not recommend using this method. If you want to set the audio profile, see \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_ac4d4cabacd4c45dcbb7439ba9d86136e}{set\+Audio\+Profile}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em fullband} & Full-\/band codec (48 k\+Hz sampling rate), not compatible with versions before v1.\+7.\+4. 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item True\+: Enable full-\/band codec. 
\item False\+: Disable full-\/band codec. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em stereo} & Stereo codec, not compatible with versions before v1.\+7.\+4. 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item True\+: Enable stereo codec. 
\item False\+: Disable stereo codec. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em full\+Bitrate} & High bitrate. Recommended in voice-\/only mode. 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item True\+: Enable high bitrate mode. 
\item False\+: Disable high bitrate mode. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success. 
\item $<$0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

Enables the {\ttfamily on\+Audio\+Volume\+Indication} callback to report on which users are speaking and the speakers\textquotesingle{} volume.

Once the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a6b9a1f4de49ef268b2be15b269ee7c47}{on\+Audio\+Volume\+Indication}} callback is enabled, the S\+DK returns the volume indication in the at the time interval set in {\ttfamily enable\+Audio\+Volume\+Indication}, regardless of whether any user is speaking in the channel.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item $<$= 0\+: Disables the volume indication.
\item $>$ 0\+: Time interval (ms) between two consecutive volume indications, and should be integral multiple of 200 (less than 200 will be set to 200). 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em smooth} & The smoothing factor that sets the sensitivity of the audio volume indicator. The value ranges is \mbox{[}0, 10\mbox{]}. The greater the value, the more sensitive the indicator. The recommended value is 3.\\

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enableLocalAudio()}{enableLocalAudio()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+enable\+Local\+Audio (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{boolean}]{enabled }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Enables or disables the local audio capture.

The audio function is enabled by default. This method disables or re-\/enables the local audio function, that is, to stop or restart local audio capture and processing.

This method does not affect receiving or playing the remote audio streams, and {\ttfamily enable\+Local\+Audio} (false) is applicable to scenarios where the user wants to receive remote audio streams without sending any audio stream to other users in the channel.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em enabled} & Determines whether to disable or re-\/enable the local audio function\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: (Default) Re-\/enable the local audio function, that is, to start local audio capture and processing.
\item false\+: Disable the local audio function, that is, to stop local audio capture and processing.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!muteAllRemoteAudioStreams@{muteAllRemoteAudioStreams}}
\index{muteAllRemoteAudioStreams@{muteAllRemoteAudioStreams}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{muteAllRemoteAudioStreams()}{muteAllRemoteAudioStreams()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{boolean}]{muted }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Stops or resumes receiving all remote audio streams.

This method works for all remote users that join or will join a channel using the {\ttfamily join\+Channel} method. It is equivalent to the {\ttfamily auto\+Subscribe\+Audio} member in the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_channel_media_options}{Channel\+Media\+Options}} class. You can call this method before, during, or after a call.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If you call {\ttfamily mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams(true)} before joining a channel, the local user does not receive any audio stream after joining the channel.
\item If you call {\ttfamily mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams(true)} after joining a channel, the local use stops receiving any audio stream from any user in the channel, including any user who joins the channel after you call this method.
\item If you call {\ttfamily mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams(true)} after leaving a channel, the local user does not receive any audio stream the next time the user joins a channel.
\end{DoxyItemize}

After you successfully call {\ttfamily mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams(true)}, you can take the following actions\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item To resume receiving all remote audio streams, call {\ttfamily mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams(false)}.
\item To resume receiving the audio stream of a specified user, call {\ttfamily mute\+Remote\+Audio\+Stream(uid, false)}, where {\ttfamily uid} is the ID of the user whose audio stream you want to resume receiving.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The result of calling this method is affected by calling {\ttfamily enable\+Audio} and {\ttfamily disable\+Audio}. Settings in {\ttfamily mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams} stop taking effect if either of the following occurs\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Calling {\ttfamily enable\+Audio} after {\ttfamily mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams(true)}.
\item Calling {\ttfamily disable\+Audio} after {\ttfamily mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams(false)}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item This method only works for the channel created by calling {\ttfamily join\+Channel}. To set whether to receive remote audio streams for a specific channel, Agora recommends using {\ttfamily auto\+Subscribe\+Audio} in the {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_channel_media_options}{Channel\+Media\+Options}}} class.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em muted} & Whether to stop receiving remote audio streams\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: Stop receiving any remote audio stream.
\item false\+: (Default) Resume receiving all remote audio streams.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a46f0ed8e5ce8d6ee962b43b434c5f70a}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a46f0ed8e5ce8d6ee962b43b434c5f70a}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!setDefaultMuteAllRemoteAudioStreams@{setDefaultMuteAllRemoteAudioStreams}}
\index{setDefaultMuteAllRemoteAudioStreams@{setDefaultMuteAllRemoteAudioStreams}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setDefaultMuteAllRemoteAudioStreams()}{setDefaultMuteAllRemoteAudioStreams()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Default\+Mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{boolean}]{muted }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Determines whether to receive all remote audio streams by default.

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000026}{Deprecated}}]This method is deprecated. To set whether to receive remote audio streams by default, call \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a300aaecf6aba89a95005d3ad6e7957b9}{mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams}} before calling {\ttfamily join\+Channel}.\end{DoxyRefDesc}


Use {\ttfamily set\+Default\+Mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams} to set whether to receive audio streams of subsequent peer users. Agora recommends calling it before joining a channel.

A successful call of {\ttfamily set\+Default\+Mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams(true)} results in that the local user not receiving any audio stream after joining a channel.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em muted} & Whether to receive remote audio streams by default\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: Do not receive any remote audio stream by default.
\item false\+: (Default)) Receive remote audio streams by default.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\

\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!enableVideo@{enableVideo}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enableVideo()}{enableVideo()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+enable\+Video (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Enables the video.

You can call this method either before joining a channel or during a call. If you call this method before entering a channel, the service starts the video; if you call it during a call, the audio call switches to a video call.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This method controls the underlying states of the Engine. It is still valid after one leaves the channel.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

Disables the video.

This method stops capturing the local video and receiving any remote video. To enable the local preview function, call \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a80351723711a6f3a66abcc287154eb10}{enable\+Local\+Video}} (true). \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_abedf2a04d1b79acd49cf9c3fcd5d8dcc}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_abedf2a04d1b79acd49cf9c3fcd5d8dcc}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!setVideoProfile@{setVideoProfile}}
\index{setVideoProfile@{setVideoProfile}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setVideoProfile()}{setVideoProfile()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Video\+Profile (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{profile,  }\item[{boolean}]{swap\+Width\+And\+Height }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets the video encoding profile.

Each profile includes a set of parameters, such as the resolution, frame rate, and bitrate. When the camera does not support the specified resolution, the S\+DK chooses a suitable camera resolution, while the encoder resolution is the one specified by \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_abedf2a04d1b79acd49cf9c3fcd5d8dcc}{set\+Video\+Profile}}.

Note\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Always set the video profile after calling the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a7146c53b6fe50980242bdd8dcddf177f}{enable\+Video}} method. 
\item Always set the video profile before calling the \mbox{\hyperlink{}{token, java.\+lang.\+String channel\+Name, java.\+lang.\+String optional\+Info, int optional\+Uid) join\+Channel}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a316bdab24f10e892955571788bbaccc2}{start\+Preview}} method. 
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em profile} & \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_1_1_video_profile}{Video\+Profile}}. \\
\hline
{\em swap\+Width\+And\+Height} & The width and height of the output video is consistent with that of the video profile you set. This parameter sets whether to swap the width and height of the stream\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item True\+: Swap the width and height. After that the video will be in the portrait mode, that is, width $<$ height. 
\item False\+: (Default) Do not swap the width and height, and the video remains in the landscape mode, that is, width $>$ height. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success. 
\item $<$0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a33af5b77701edea3f565e05e2bd7e9d4}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a33af5b77701edea3f565e05e2bd7e9d4}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!setVideoEncoderConfiguration@{setVideoEncoderConfiguration}}
\index{setVideoEncoderConfiguration@{setVideoEncoderConfiguration}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setVideoEncoderConfiguration()}{setVideoEncoderConfiguration()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Video\+Encoder\+Configuration (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1video_1_1_video_encoder_configuration}{Video\+Encoder\+Configuration}}}]{config }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets the video encoder configuration.

Each configuration profile corresponds to a set of video parameters, including the resolution, frame rate, and bitrate.

The parameters specified in this method are the maximum values under ideal network conditions. If the video engine cannot render the video using the specified parameters due to poor network conditions, the parameters further down the list are considered until a successful configuration is found.

{\em config} & The local video encoder configuration\+: Video\+Encoder\+Configuration. \\

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setupLocalVideo()}{setupLocalVideo()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+setup\+Local\+Video (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1video_1_1_video_canvas}{Video\+Canvas}}}]{local }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Initializes the local video view.

This method initializes the video view of the local stream on the local device. It affects only the video view that the local user sees, not the published local video stream.

To unbind the local video from the view, set {\ttfamily view} in Video\+Canvas as {\ttfamily null}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Call this method before joining a channel.
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!setupRemoteVideo@{setupRemoteVideo}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setupRemoteVideo()}{setupRemoteVideo()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+setup\+Remote\+Video (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1video_1_1_video_canvas}{Video\+Canvas}}}]{remote }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Initializes the video view of a remote user.

This method initializes the video view of a remote stream on the local device. It affects only the video view that the local user sees.

Usually the app should specify the {\ttfamily uid} of the remote video in the method call before the remote user joins the channel. If the remote {\ttfamily uid} is unknown to the app, set it later when the app receives the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a848d29acef97523964bb27dd5b637162}{on\+User\+Joined}} callback.

To unbind the remote user from the view, set {\ttfamily view} in Video\+Canvas as {\ttfamily null}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Ensure that you call this method in the UI thread.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em remote} & The remote video view settings\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1video_1_1_video_canvas}{Video\+Canvas}}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setLocalRenderMode()}{setLocalRenderMode()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Local\+Render\+Mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{render\+Mode }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Updates the display mode of the local video view.

After initializing the local video view, you can call this method to update its rendering mode. It affects only the video view that the local user sees, not the published local video stream.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Ensure that you have called \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a75485acddd3d8593f8a7403c489c9d7f}{setup\+Local\+Video}} to initialize the local video view before this method.
\item During a call, you can call this method as many times as necessary to update the local video view.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em render\+Mode} & Sets the local display mode\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily R\+E\+N\+D\+E\+R\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+H\+I\+D\+D\+EN}(1)\+: Uniformly scale the video until it fills the visible boundaries (cropped). One dimension of the video may have clipped contents.
\item {\ttfamily R\+E\+N\+D\+E\+R\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+F\+IT}(2)\+: Uniformly scale the video until one of its dimension fits the boundary (zoomed to fit). Areas that are not filled due to the disparity in the aspect ratio will be filled with black.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

Creates a video renderer view. \begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000027}{Deprecated}}]This method is deprecated. You can use Surface\+View or Texture\+View created by Android system. \end{DoxyRefDesc}


It returns the \mbox{\hyperlink{}{Surface\+View}} type. The operation and layout of the view are managed by the application, and the Agora S\+DK renders the view provided by the application. The view to display videos must be created using this method instead of directly calling \mbox{\hyperlink{}{Surface\+View}}.

Starts the local video preview before joining a channel.

Once you call this method to start the local video preview, if you leave the channel by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_af3fe5d61a9ca8db36b56432273d02307}{leave\+Channel}}, the local video preview remains until you call \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a2b6f702ce3e43c943836a9dce514a129}{stop\+Preview}} to disable it.

\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!enableLocalVideo@{enableLocalVideo}}
\index{enableLocalVideo@{enableLocalVideo}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enableLocalVideo()}{enableLocalVideo()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+enable\+Local\+Video (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{boolean}]{enabled }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Disables or re-\/enables the local video capture.

Once you enable the video using \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a7146c53b6fe50980242bdd8dcddf177f}{enable\+Video}}, the local video is enabled by default. This method disables or re-\/enables the local video capture.

{\ttfamily enable\+Local\+Video(false)} applies to scenarios when the user wants to watch the remote video without sending any video stream to the other user.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Call this method after {\ttfamily enable\+Video}. Otherwise, this method may not work properly.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em enabled} & Determines whether to disable or re-\/enable the local video, including the capturer, renderer, and sender\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: (Default) Re-\/enable the local video.
\item false\+: Disable the local video. Once the local video is disabled, the remote users can no longer receive the video stream of this user, while this user can still receive the video streams of other remote users. When you set {\ttfamily enabled} as {\ttfamily false}, this method does not require a local camera.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+mute\+Remote\+Video\+Stream (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{user\+Id,  }\item[{boolean}]{muted }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_aae74ecd1bf61812930605994bd1bb77c}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_aae74ecd1bf61812930605994bd1bb77c}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!muteAllRemoteVideoStreams@{muteAllRemoteVideoStreams}}
\index{muteAllRemoteVideoStreams@{muteAllRemoteVideoStreams}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{muteAllRemoteVideoStreams()}{muteAllRemoteVideoStreams()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{boolean}]{muted }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Stops or resumes receiving all remote video streams.

This method works for all remote users that join or will join a channel using the {\ttfamily join\+Channel} method. It is equivalent to the {\ttfamily auto\+Subscribe\+Video} member in the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_channel_media_options}{Channel\+Media\+Options}} class. You can call this method before, during, or after a call.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If you call {\ttfamily mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams(true)} before joining a channel, the local user does not receive any video stream after joining the channel.
\item If you call {\ttfamily mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams(true)} after joining a channel, the local use stops receiving any video stream from any user in the channel, including any user who joins the channel after you call this method.
\item If you call {\ttfamily mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams(true)} after leaving a channel, the local user does not receive any video stream the next time the user joins a channel.
\end{DoxyItemize}

After you successfully call {\ttfamily mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams(true)}, you can take the following actions\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item To resume receiving all remote video streams, call {\ttfamily mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams(false)}.
\item To resume receiving the video stream of a specified user, call {\ttfamily mute\+Remote\+Video\+Stream(uid, false)}, where {\ttfamily uid} is the ID of the user whose video stream you want to resume receiving.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The result of calling this method is affected by calling {\ttfamily enable\+Video} and {\ttfamily disable\+Video}. Settings in {\ttfamily mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams} stop taking effect if either of the following occurs\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Calling {\ttfamily enable\+Video} after {\ttfamily mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams(true)}.
\item Calling {\ttfamily disable\+Video} after {\ttfamily mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams(false)}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item This method only works for the channel created by calling {\ttfamily join\+Channel}. To set whether to receive remote audio streams for a specific channel, Agora recommends using {\ttfamily auto\+Subscribe\+Video} in the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_channel_media_options}{Channel\+Media\+Options}} class.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em muted} & Whether to stop receiving remote video streams\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: Stop receiving any remote video stream.
\item false\+: (Default) R\+Resume receiving all remote video streams.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_aaf7c2c265dcc72657aa4d2320f871ee0}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_aaf7c2c265dcc72657aa4d2320f871ee0}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!setDefaultMuteAllRemoteVideoStreams@{setDefaultMuteAllRemoteVideoStreams}}
\index{setDefaultMuteAllRemoteVideoStreams@{setDefaultMuteAllRemoteVideoStreams}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setDefaultMuteAllRemoteVideoStreams()}{setDefaultMuteAllRemoteVideoStreams()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Default\+Mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{boolean}]{muted }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Determines whether to receive all remote video streams by default.

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000029}{Deprecated}}]This method is deprecated. To set whether to receive remote video streams by default, call \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_aae74ecd1bf61812930605994bd1bb77c}{mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams}} before calling {\ttfamily join\+Channel}.\end{DoxyRefDesc}


Use {\ttfamily set\+Default\+Mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams} to set whether to receive video streams of subsequent peer users. Agora recommends calling it before joining a channel.

A successful call of {\ttfamily set\+Default\+Mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams(true)} results in that the local user not receiving any video stream after joining a channel.

\item false\+: (Default) Receive remote video streams by default.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setLowlightEnhanceOptions()}{setLowlightEnhanceOptions()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Lowlight\+Enhance\+Options (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{boolean}]{enabled,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1video_1_1_low_light_enhance_options}{Low\+Light\+Enhance\+Options}}}]{options }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets low-\/light enhancement.

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
v3.\+6.\+2
\end{DoxySince}
The low-\/light enhancement feature can adaptively adjust the brightness value of the video captured in situations with low or uneven lighting, such as backlit, cloudy, or dark scenes. It restores or highlights the image details and improves the overall visual effect of the video.

You can call this method to enable the low-\/light enhancement feature and set the options of the low-\/light enhancement effect.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Before calling this method, ensure that you have integrated the {\ttfamily libagora\+\_\+clear\+\_\+vision\+\_\+extension.\+so} dynamic library.
\item Call this method after \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a7146c53b6fe50980242bdd8dcddf177f}{enable\+Video}}.
\item The low-\/light enhancement feature has certain performance requirements on devices. If your device overheats after you enable low-\/light enhancement, Agora recommends modifying the low-\/light enhancement options to a less performance-\/consuming level or disabling low-\/light enhancement entirely.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em enabled} & Sets whether to enable low-\/light enhancement\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily true}\+: Enable.
\item {\ttfamily false}\+: (Default) Disable. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em options} & The low-\/light enhancement options. See \{\mbox{\hyperlink{}{Low\+Light\+Enhance\+Options\}. 0\+: Success.$<$ 0\+: Failure. }}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Sets video noise reduction.

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
v3.\+6.\+2
\end{DoxySince}
Underlit environments and low-\/end video capture devices can cause video images to contain significant noise, which affects video quality. In real-\/time interactive scenarios, video noise also consumes bitstream resources and reduces encoding efficiency during encoding.

You can call this method to enable the video noise reduction feature and set the options of the video noise reduction effect.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Before calling this method, ensure that you have integrated the {\ttfamily libagora\+\_\+clear\+\_\+vision\+\_\+extension.\+so} dynamic library.
\item Call this method after \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a7146c53b6fe50980242bdd8dcddf177f}{enable\+Video}}.
\item The video noise reduction feature has certain performance requirements on devices. If your device overheats after you enable video noise reduction, Agora recommends modifying the video noise reduction options to a less performance-\/consuming level or disabling video noise reduction entirely.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

Sets color enhancement.

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
v3.\+6.\+2
\end{DoxySince}
The video images captured by the camera can have color distortion. The color enhancement feature intelligently adjusts video characteristics such as saturation and contrast to enhance the video color richness and color reproduction, making the video more vivid.

You can call this method to enable the color enhancement feature and set the options of the color enhancement effect.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}

\item The color enhancement feature has certain performance requirements on devices. If your device overheats after you enable color enhancement, Agora recommends modifying the color enhancement options to a less performance-\/consuming level or disabling color enhancement entirely.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!enableRemoteSuperResolution@{enableRemoteSuperResolution}}
\index{enableRemoteSuperResolution@{enableRemoteSuperResolution}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enableRemoteSuperResolution()}{enableRemoteSuperResolution()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+enable\+Remote\+Super\+Resolution (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{uid,  }\item[{boolean}]{enable }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Enables/\+Disables the super resolution feature for a remote user\textquotesingle{}s video. (beta feature)

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
v4.\+0.\+0
\end{DoxySince}
This feature effectively boosts the resolution of a remote user\textquotesingle{}s video seen by the local user. If the original resolution of a remote user\textquotesingle{}s video is a  b, the local user\textquotesingle{}s device can render the remote video at a resolution of 2a  2b after you enable this feature.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
The super resolution feature requires extra system resources. To balance the visual experience and system consumption, the S\+DK poses the following restrictions\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This feature can only be enabled for a single remote user.
\item The original resolution of the remote user\textquotesingle{}s video cannot exceed a certain range. If the local user use super resolution on Android, the original resolution of the remote user\textquotesingle{}s video cannot exceed 640  360 pixels; if the local user use super resolution on i\+OS, the original resolution of the remote user\textquotesingle{}s video cannot exceed 640  480 pixels.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This method is for Android and i\+OS only.
\item Before calling this method, ensure that you have integrated the following dynamic library into your project\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Android\+: {\ttfamily libagora\+\_\+super\+\_\+resolution\+\_\+extension.\+so}
\item i\+OS\+: {\ttfamily Agora\+Super\+Resolution\+Extension.\+xcframework}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Because this method has certain system performance requirements, Agora recommends that you use the following devices or better\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Android\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item V\+I\+VO\+: V1821A, N\+EX S, 1914A, 1916A, 1962A, 1824BA, X60, X60 Pro
\item O\+P\+PO\+: P\+C\+C\+M00, Find X3
\item One\+Plus\+: A6000
\item Xiaomi\+: Mi 8, Mi 9, Mi 10, Mi 11, M\+I\+X3, Redmi K20 Pro
\item S\+A\+M\+S\+U\+NG\+: S\+M-\/\+G9600, S\+M-\/\+G9650, S\+M-\/\+N9600, S\+M-\/\+G9708, S\+M-\/\+G960U, S\+M-\/\+G9750, S20, S21
\item H\+U\+A\+W\+EI\+: S\+E\+A-\/\+A\+L00, E\+L\+E-\/\+A\+L00, V\+O\+G-\/\+A\+L00, Y\+A\+L-\/\+A\+L10, H\+M\+A-\/\+A\+L00, E\+V\+R-\/\+A\+N00, nova 4, nova 5 Pro, nova 6 5G, nova 7 5G, Mate 30, Mate 30 Pro, Mate 40, Mate 40 Pro, P40 P40 Pro, H\+U\+A\+W\+EI Media\+Pad M6, Mate\+Pad 10.\+8
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!setDefaultAudioRoutetoSpeakerphone@{setDefaultAudioRoutetoSpeakerphone}}
\index{setDefaultAudioRoutetoSpeakerphone@{setDefaultAudioRoutetoSpeakerphone}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setDefaultAudioRoutetoSpeakerphone()}{setDefaultAudioRoutetoSpeakerphone()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Default\+Audio\+Routeto\+Speakerphone (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{boolean}]{default\+To\+Speaker }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets the default audio route.

Most mobile phones have two audio routes\+: an earpiece at the top, and a speakerphone at the bottom. The earpiece plays at a lower volume, and the speakerphone at a higher volume.

When setting the default audio route, you determine whether audio playback comes through the earpiece or speakerphone when no external audio device is connected.

Depending on the scenario, Agora uses different default audio routes\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Voice call\+: Earpiece.
\item Video call\+: Speakerphone.
\item Audio broadcast\+: Speakerphone.
\item Video broadcast\+: Speakerphone.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Call this method before, during, or after a call, to change the default audio route. When the audio route changes, the S\+DK triggers the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a9685280586a4fce917eac08257fdeaf9}{on\+Audio\+Route\+Changed}} callback.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The system audio route changes when an external audio device, such as a headphone or a Bluetooth audio device, is connected. See {\itshape Principles for Changing the Audio Route}.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em default\+To\+Speaker} & Whether to set the speakerphone as the default audio route\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: Set the speakerphone as the default audio route.
\item false\+: Do not set the speakerphone as the default audio route. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a5dce9e487806eb87da6c142450498f61}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a5dce9e487806eb87da6c142450498f61}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!setEnableSpeakerphone@{setEnableSpeakerphone}}
\index{setEnableSpeakerphone@{setEnableSpeakerphone}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setEnableSpeakerphone()}{setEnableSpeakerphone()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Enable\+Speakerphone (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{boolean}]{enabled }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Enables or disables the speakerphone temporarily.

When the audio route changes, the S\+DK triggers the \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a9685280586a4fce917eac08257fdeaf9}{on\+Audio\+Route\+Changed\} callback. You can call this method before, during, or after a call. However, Agora recommends calling this method only when you are in a channel to change the audio route temporarily.  This method sets the audio route temporarily. Plugging in or unplugging a headphone, or the S\+DK re-\/enabling the audio device module (A\+DM) to adjust the media volume in some scenarios relating to audio, leads to a change in the audio route. See {\itshape Principles for Changing the Audio Route}.  enabled Whether to set the speakerphone as the temporary audio route\+:true\+: Set the speakerphone as the audio route temporarily.false\+: Do not set the speakerphone as the audio route. 0\+: Success.$<$0\+: Failure. }}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_ae5916d5e8b659ef49a8c1ec9ff54d8dc}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_ae5916d5e8b659ef49a8c1ec9ff54d8dc}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setHeadphoneEQParameters()}{setHeadphoneEQParameters()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Headphone\+E\+Q\+Parameters (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{float}]{low\+\_\+gain,  }\item[{float}]{high\+\_\+gain }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets the parameters of audio playback effect for remote headphones after remote audio is mixed.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em low\+\_\+gain} & The higher the parameter value, the deeper the sound. The value range is \mbox{[}-\/1.\+0,1.\+0\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
{\em high\+\_\+gain} & The higher the parameter value, the sharper the sound. The value range is \mbox{[}-\/1.\+0,1.\+0\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item -\/1(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED)\+: A general error occurs (no specified reason). 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a9f13e2709b7d084ff351c9506d6446d0}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a9f13e2709b7d084ff351c9506d6446d0}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!setAudioEffectPreset@{setAudioEffectPreset}}
\index{setAudioEffectPreset@{setAudioEffectPreset}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setAudioEffectPreset()}{setAudioEffectPreset()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Audio\+Effect\+Preset (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{preset }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets an S\+DK preset audio effect.

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
v3.\+2.\+0
\end{DoxySince}
Call this method to set an S\+DK preset audio effect for the local user who sends an audio stream. This audio effect does not change the gender characteristics of the original voice. After setting an audio effect, all users in the channel can hear the effect.

You can set different audio effects for different scenarios. See {\itshape Set the Voice Effect}.

To achieve better audio effect quality, Agora recommends calling \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_abb4b63716fda137ecd5254137c79547f}{set\+Audio\+Profile\} and setting the {\ttfamily scenario} parameter to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+S\+C\+E\+N\+A\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+I\+N\+G(3)} before calling this method. You can call this method either before or after joining a channel.Do not set the profile parameter of {\ttfamily set\+Audio\+Profile} to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+P\+E\+E\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+N\+D\+A\+R\+D(1)}; otherwise, this method call does not take effect.This method works best with the human voice. Agora does not recommend using this method for audio containing music.If you call this method and set the preset parameter to enumerators except {\ttfamily R\+O\+O\+M\+\_\+\+A\+C\+O\+U\+S\+T\+I\+C\+S\+\_\+3\+D\+\_\+\+V\+O\+I\+CE} or {\ttfamily P\+I\+T\+C\+H\+\_\+\+C\+O\+R\+R\+E\+C\+T\+I\+ON}, do not call  set\+Audio\+Effect\+Parameters set\+Audio\+Effect\+Parameters\}; otherwise, {\ttfamily set\+Audio\+Effect\+Parameters} overrides this method.After calling this method, Agora recommends not calling the following methods, because they can override {\ttfamily set\+Audio\+Effect\+Preset}\+:  Rtc\+Engine\#set\+Voice\+Beautifier\+Preset set\+Voice\+Beautifier\+Preset\} Rtc\+Engine\#set\+Local\+Voice\+Pitch set\+Local\+Voice\+Pitch\} Rtc\+Engine\#set\+Local\+Voice\+Equalization set\+Local\+Voice\+Equalization\} Rtc\+Engine\#set\+Local\+Voice\+Reverb set\+Local\+Voice\+Reverb\}
