Sets an S\+DK preset voice beautifier effect.

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
v3.\+2.\+0
\end{DoxySince}
Call this method to set an S\+DK preset voice beautifier effect for the local user who sends an audio stream. After setting a voice beautifier effect, all users in the channel can hear the effect.

You can set different voice beautifier effects for different scenarios. See {\itshape Set the Voice Effect}.

To achieve better audio effect quality, Agora recommends calling \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_abb4b63716fda137ecd5254137c79547f}{set\+Audio\+Profile\} and setting the {\ttfamily scenario} parameter to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+S\+C\+E\+N\+A\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+I\+N\+G(3)} and the {\ttfamily profile} parameter to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y(4)} or {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+E\+R\+E\+O(5)} before calling this method. You can call this method either before or after joining a channel.Do not set the profile parameter of {\ttfamily set\+Audio\+Profile} to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+P\+E\+E\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+N\+D\+A\+R\+D(1)}; otherwise, this method call does not take effect.This method works best with the human voice. {\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Voice\+Conversion\+Preset (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{preset }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets an S\+DK preset voice conversion effect.

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
v3.\+3.\+1
\end{DoxySince}
Call this method to set an S\+DK preset voice conversion effect for the local user who sends an audio stream. After setting a voice conversion effect, all users in the channel can hear the effect.

You can set different voice conversion effects for different scenarios. See {\itshape Set the Voice Effect}.

To achieve better audio effect quality, Agora recommends calling \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_abb4b63716fda137ecd5254137c79547f}{set\+Audio\+Profile\} and setting the {\ttfamily scenario} parameter to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+S\+C\+E\+N\+A\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+I\+N\+G(3)} and the {\ttfamily profile} parameter to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y(4)} or {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+E\+R\+E\+O(5)} before calling this method. You can call this method either before or after joining a channel.Do not set the {\ttfamily profile} parameter of {\ttfamily set\+Audio\+Profile} to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+P\+E\+E\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+N\+D\+A\+R\+D(1)}; otherwise, this method call does not take effect.This method works best with the human voice. \index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!setAudioEffectParameters@{setAudioEffectParameters}}
\index{setAudioEffectParameters@{setAudioEffectParameters}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setAudioEffectParameters()}{setAudioEffectParameters()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Audio\+Effect\+Parameters (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{preset,  }\item[{int}]{param1,  }\item[{int}]{param2 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets parameters for S\+DK preset audio effects.

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
v3.\+2.\+0
\end{DoxySince}
Call this method to set the following parameters for the local user who sends an audio stream\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 3D voice effect\+: Sets the cycle period of the 3D voice effect.
\item Pitch correction effect\+: Sets the basic mode and tonic pitch of the pitch correction effect. Different songs have different modes and tonic pitches. Agora recommends bounding this method with interface elements to enable users to adjust the pitch correction interactively.
\end{DoxyItemize}

After setting parameters, all users in the channel can hear the relevant effect.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item You can call this method either before or after joining a channel.
\item To achieve better audio effect quality, Agora recommends calling {\ttfamily set\+Audio\+Profile} and setting the scenario parameter to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+S\+C\+E\+N\+A\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+I\+N\+G(3)} before calling this method.
\item Do not set the profile parameter of set\+Audio\+Profile to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+P\+E\+E\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+N\+D\+A\+R\+D(1)}; otherwise, this method call does not take effect.
\item This method works best with the human voice. Agora does not recommend using this method for audio containing music.
\item After calling this method, Agora recommends not calling the following methods, because they can override {\ttfamily set\+Audio\+Effect\+Parameters}\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a9f13e2709b7d084ff351c9506d6446d0}{set\+Audio\+Effect\+Preset}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a5a866fbb28c34fc38c3f600f78d61e73}{set\+Voice\+Beautifier\+Preset}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a5415bac7850599bb5b620dc9c6bd4993}{set\+Local\+Voice\+Pitch}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a4e707946700a15c2b7d99177db830a54}{set\+Local\+Voice\+Equalization}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_ac955fd38973b32c629cdfa1566e52fc6}{set\+Local\+Voice\+Reverb}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_af712699445c8ff8118f5d1027dc636ca}{set\+Voice\+Beautifier\+Parameters}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_ae9cfcbcb51a1a179a2b57d0f016b400c}{set\+Voice\+Conversion\+Preset}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em preset} & The options for S\+DK preset audio effects\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 3D voice effect\+: {\ttfamily R\+O\+O\+M\+\_\+\+A\+C\+O\+U\+S\+T\+I\+C\+S\+\_\+3\+D\+\_\+\+V\+O\+I\+CE}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Call {\ttfamily set\+Audio\+Profile} and set the {\ttfamily profile} parameter to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+N\+D\+A\+R\+D\+\_\+\+S\+T\+E\+R\+E\+O(3)} or {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+E\+R\+E\+O(5)} before setting this enumerator; otherwise, the enumerator setting does not take effect.
\item If the 3D voice effect is enabled, users need to use stereo audio playback devices to hear the anticipated voice effect.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Pitch correction effect\+: {\ttfamily P\+I\+T\+C\+H\+\_\+\+C\+O\+R\+R\+E\+C\+T\+I\+ON}. To achieve better audio effect quality, Agora recommends calling {\ttfamily set\+Audio\+Profile} and setting the {\ttfamily profile} parameter to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y(4)} or {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+E\+R\+E\+O(5)} before setting this enumerator. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em param1} & 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If you set {\ttfamily preset} to {\ttfamily R\+O\+O\+M\+\_\+\+A\+C\+O\+U\+S\+T\+I\+C\+S\+\_\+3\+D\+\_\+\+V\+O\+I\+CE}, the {\ttfamily param1} sets the cycle period of the 3D voice effect. The value range is \mbox{[}1, 60\mbox{]} and the unit is a second. The default value is 10 seconds, indicating that the voice moves around you every 10 seconds.
\item If you set {\ttfamily preset} to {\ttfamily P\+I\+T\+C\+H\+\_\+\+C\+O\+R\+R\+E\+C\+T\+I\+ON}, {\ttfamily param1} sets the basic mode of the pitch correction effect\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily 1}\+: (Default) Natural major scale.
\item {\ttfamily 2}\+: Natural minor scale.
\item {\ttfamily 3}\+: Japanese pentatonic scale. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em param2} & 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item You need to set {\ttfamily param2} to {\ttfamily 0}.
\item If you set {\ttfamily preset} to {\ttfamily P\+I\+T\+C\+H\+\_\+\+C\+O\+R\+R\+E\+C\+T\+I\+ON}, {\ttfamily param2} sets the tonic pitch of the pitch correction effect\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily 1}\+: A
\item {\ttfamily 2}\+: A\#
\item {\ttfamily 3}\+: B
\item {\ttfamily 4}\+: (Default) C
\item {\ttfamily 5}\+: C\#
\item {\ttfamily 6}\+: D
\item {\ttfamily 7}\+: D\#
\item {\ttfamily 8}\+: E
\item {\ttfamily 9}\+: F
\item {\ttfamily 10}\+: F\#
\item {\ttfamily 11}\+: G
\item {\ttfamily 12}\+: G\# 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline

\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!setVoiceBeautifierParameters@{setVoiceBeautifierParameters}}
\index{setVoiceBeautifierParameters@{setVoiceBeautifierParameters}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setVoiceBeautifierParameters()}{setVoiceBeautifierParameters()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Voice\+Beautifier\+Parameters (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{preset,  }\item[{int}]{param1,  }\item[{int}]{param2 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets parameters for S\+DK preset voice beautifier effects.

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
3.\+3.\+0.
\end{DoxySince}
Call this method to set a gender characteristic and a reverberation effect for the singing beautifier effect. This method sets parameters for the local user who sends an audio stream.

After you call this method successfully, all users in the channel can hear the relevant effect.

To achieve better audio effect quality, before you call this method, Agora recommends calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_abb4b63716fda137ecd5254137c79547f}{set\+Audio\+Profile}}, and setting the scenario parameter to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+S\+C\+E\+N\+A\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+I\+N\+G(3)} and the profile parameter to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y(4)} or {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+E\+R\+E\+O(5)}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item You can call this method either before or after joining a channel.
\item Do not set the {\ttfamily profile} parameter of {\ttfamily set\+Audio\+Profile} to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+P\+E\+E\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+N\+D\+A\+R\+D(1)}; otherwise, this method call does not take effect.
\item This method works best with the human voice. Agora does not recommend using this method for audio containing music.
\item After you call this method, Agora recommends not calling the following methods, because they can override {\ttfamily set\+Voice\+Beautifier\+Parameters}\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a9f13e2709b7d084ff351c9506d6446d0}{set\+Audio\+Effect\+Preset}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_aaf70d13931b9a2194cd96284b37dc071}{set\+Audio\+Effect\+Parameters}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a5a866fbb28c34fc38c3f600f78d61e73}{set\+Voice\+Beautifier\+Preset}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a5415bac7850599bb5b620dc9c6bd4993}{set\+Local\+Voice\+Pitch}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a4e707946700a15c2b7d99177db830a54}{set\+Local\+Voice\+Equalization}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_ac955fd38973b32c629cdfa1566e52fc6}{set\+Local\+Voice\+Reverb}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_ae9cfcbcb51a1a179a2b57d0f016b400c}{set\+Voice\+Conversion\+Preset}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em preset} & The options for S\+DK preset voice beautifier effects\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily S\+I\+N\+G\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+B\+E\+A\+U\+T\+I\+F\+I\+ER}\+: Singing beautifier effect. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em param1} & The gender characteristics options for the singing voice\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}

\item {\ttfamily 2}\+: A female-\/sounding voice. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily 1}\+: The reverberation effect sounds like singing in a small room.
\item {\ttfamily 2}\+: The reverberation effect sounds like singing in a large room.
\item {\ttfamily 3}\+: The reverberation effect sounds like singing in a hall. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enableSoundPositionIndication()}{enableSoundPositionIndication()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+enable\+Sound\+Position\+Indication (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{boolean}]{enabled }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Enables/\+Disables stereo panning for remote users. Ensure that you call this method before join\+Channel to enable stereo panning for remote users so that the local user can track the position of a remote user by calling set\+Remote\+Voice\+Position. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: enables stereo panning.
\item false\+: disables stereo panning. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_acf43fddf9cb4e3b76f5407ff6f6d57a4}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_acf43fddf9cb4e3b76f5407ff6f6d57a4}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!setRemoteVoicePosition@{setRemoteVoicePosition}}
\index{setRemoteVoicePosition@{setRemoteVoicePosition}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setRemoteVoicePosition()}{setRemoteVoicePosition()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Remote\+Voice\+Position (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{uid,  }\item[{double}]{pan,  }\item[{double}]{gain }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets the sound position and gain of a remote user. When the local user calls this method to set the sound position of a remote user, the sound difference between the left and right channels allows the local user to track the real-\/time position of the remote user, creating a real sense of space. This method applies to massively multiplayer online games, such as Battle Royale games. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item For this method to work, enable stereo panning for remote users by calling the enable\+Sound\+Position\+Indication method before joining a channel.
\item This method requires hardware support. For the best sound positioning, we recommend using a wired headset.
\item Ensure that you call this method after joining a channel. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em uid} & The ID of the remote user. \\
\hline
{\em pan} & The sound position of the remote user. The value ranges from -\/1.\+0 to 1.\+0\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0.\+0\+: the remote sound comes from the front.
\item -\/1.\+0\+: the remote sound comes from the left.
\item 1.\+0\+: the remote sound comes from the right. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em gain} & Gain of the remote user. The value ranges from 0.\+0 to 100.\+0. The default value is 100.\+0 (the original gain of the remote user). The smaller the value, the less the gain. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a18c4fcacfc39625ae8a47e66564bd8f4}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a18c4fcacfc39625ae8a47e66564bd8f4}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!startAudioMixing@{startAudioMixing}}
\index{startAudioMixing@{startAudioMixing}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{startAudioMixing()}{startAudioMixing()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+start\+Audio\+Mixing (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{file\+Path,  }\item[{boolean}]{loopback,  }\item[{int}]{cycle }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Starts playing and mixing the music file.

This method mixes the specified local or online audio file with the audio stream from the microphone, or replaces the microphones audio stream with the specified local or remote audio file.

You can choose whether the other user can hear the local audio playback and specify the number of playback loops.

A successful {\ttfamily start\+Audio\+Mixing} method call triggers the \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_aad11908ae1e0b8447b13e20989f334d2}{on\+Audio\+Mixing\+State\+Changed\}(A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+X\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+L\+A\+Y\+I\+NG) callback on the local client. When the audio mixing file playback finishes, the S\+DK triggers the \{ I\+Rtc\+Engine\+Event\+Handler\#on\+Audio\+Mixing\+State\+Changed on\+Audio\+Mixing\+State\+Changed\}(A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+X\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+S\+T\+O\+P\+P\+ED) callback on the local client.  file\+Path Specifies the absolute path (including the suffixes of the filename) of the local or online audio file to be mixed. For example, {\ttfamily /sdcard/emulated/0/audio.mp4}. Supported audio formats\+: mp3, mp4, m4a, aac, 3gp, mkv, and wav.If the path begins with /assets/, the audio file is in the /assets/ directory.Otherwise, the audio file is in the absolute path.  loopback Sets which user can hear the audio mixing\+:true\+: Only the local user can hear the audio mixing.false\+: Both users can hear the audio mixing.  cycle Sets the number of playback loops\+:Positive integer\+: Number of playback loops.-\/1\+: Infinite playback loops. To use this method, ensure that the Android device is v4.\+2 or later, and the A\+PI version is v16 or later.Call this method when you are in the channel, otherwise it may cause issues.If you want to play an online music file, ensure that the time interval between calling this method is more than 100 ms, or the {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+P\+E\+N\+\_\+\+T\+O\+O\+\_\+\+F\+R\+E\+Q\+U\+E\+N\+T(702)} warning occurs.If you want to play an online music file, Agora does not recommend using the redirected U\+RL address. Some Android devices may fail to open a redirected U\+RL address.If you call this method on an emulator, only the M\+P3 file format is supported. 0\+: Success.$<$ 0\+: Failure. Constants\#\+W\+A\+R\+N\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+X\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+O\+P\+E\+N\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR W\+A\+R\+N\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+X\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+O\+P\+E\+N\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR (701)\}\+: If the local audio file does not exist, or the online audio packet is not received within five seconds after it is opened, the S\+DK assumes that the media file cannot be used and returns this warning. }}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a47d69cd55bd3ec87dfec7060c7b9b045}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a47d69cd55bd3ec87dfec7060c7b9b045}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!startAudioMixing@{startAudioMixing}}
\index{startAudioMixing@{startAudioMixing}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{startAudioMixing()}{startAudioMixing()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+start\+Audio\+Mixing (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{file\+Path,  }\item[{boolean}]{loopback,  }\item[{int}]{cycle,  }\item[{int}]{start\+Pos }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Starts playing and mixing the music file.

This method mixes the specified local or online audio file with the audio stream from the microphone, or replaces the microphones audio stream with the specified local or remote audio file.

You can choose whether the other user can hear the local audio playback and specify the number of playback loops.

A successful {\ttfamily start\+Audio\+Mixing} method call triggers the \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_aad11908ae1e0b8447b13e20989f334d2}{on\+Audio\+Mixing\+State\+Changed\}(A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+X\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+L\+A\+Y\+I\+NG) callback on the local client. When the audio mixing file playback finishes, the S\+DK triggers the \{ I\+Rtc\+Engine\+Event\+Handler\#on\+Audio\+Mixing\+State\+Changed on\+Audio\+Mixing\+State\+Changed\}(A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+X\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+S\+T\+O\+P\+P\+ED) callback on the local client.  file\+Path Specifies the absolute path (including the suffixes of the filename) of the local or online audio file to be mixed. For example, {\ttfamily /sdcard/emulated/0/audio.mp4}. Supported audio formats\+: mp3, mp4, m4a, aac, 3gp, mkv, and wav.If the path begins with /assets/, the audio file is in the /assets/ directory.Otherwise, the audio file is in the absolute path.  loopback Sets which user can hear the audio mixing\+:true\+: Only the local user can hear the audio mixing.false\+: Both users can hear the audio mixing.  cycle Sets the number of playback loops\+:Positive integer\+: Number of playback loops.-\/1\+: Infinite playback loops.  start\+Pos The playback position (ms) of the music file. To use this method, ensure that the Android device is v4.\+2 or later, and the A\+PI version is v16 or later.Call this method when you are in the channel, otherwise it may cause issues.If you want to play an online music file, ensure that the time interval between calling this method is more than 100 ms, or the {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+P\+E\+N\+\_\+\+T\+O\+O\+\_\+\+F\+R\+E\+Q\+U\+E\+N\+T(702)} warning occurs.If you want to play an online music file, Agora does not recommend using the redirected U\+RL address. Some Android devices may fail to open a redirected U\+RL address.If you call this method on an emulator, only the M\+P3 file format is supported. 0\+: Success.$<$ 0\+: Failure. Constants\#\+W\+A\+R\+N\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+X\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+O\+P\+E\+N\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR W\+A\+R\+N\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+X\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+O\+P\+E\+N\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR (701)\}\+: If the local audio file does not exist, or the online audio packet is not received within five seconds after it is opened, the S\+DK assumes that the media file cannot be used and returns this warning. }}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a8d9f13f4f48f9a2737a27c1b55ac6145}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a8d9f13f4f48f9a2737a27c1b55ac6145}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a8a868bc783c424a88c02fee7e9d4dbed}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a8a868bc783c424a88c02fee7e9d4dbed}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!startAudioRecording@{startAudioRecording}}
\index{startAudioRecording@{startAudioRecording}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{startAudioRecording()}{startAudioRecording()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+start\+Audio\+Recording (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{file\+Path,  }\item[{int}]{quality }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Starts an audio recording.

The S\+DK allows recording during a call, which supports either one of the following formats\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item .wav\+: Large file size with high sound fidelity 
\item .aac\+: Small file size with low sound fidelity 
\end{DoxyItemize}

Ensure that the directory to save the recording file exists and is writable. This method is usually called after the \mbox{\hyperlink{}{token, java.\+lang.\+String channel\+Name, java.\+lang.\+String optional\+Info, int optional\+Uid) join\+Channel}} method. The recording automatically stops when the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_af3fe5d61a9ca8db36b56432273d02307}{leave\+Channel}} method is called.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em file\+Path} & Full file path of the recording file. The string of the file name is in U\+T\+F-\/8 code. \\
\hline
{\em quality} & Audio recording quality\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_ac9a1bb3cc2d54a36332fcbad0f3010e9}{A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+R\+E\+C\+O\+R\+D\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+L\+O\+W(0)}} 
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_a47fdcd11b12d84dbdc9e5f32d7dddae2}{A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+R\+E\+C\+O\+R\+D\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+M\+E\+D\+I\+U\+M(1)}} 
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_a9d5dc7cca98bb4d0d86b7f634b5c5e0c}{A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+R\+E\+C\+O\+R\+D\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H(2)}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success. 
\item $<$0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_aedb9b84a3afd1c5b7316112710b21d8f}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_aedb9b84a3afd1c5b7316112710b21d8f}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!startAudioRecording@{startAudioRecording}}
\index{startAudioRecording@{startAudioRecording}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{startAudioRecording()}{startAudioRecording()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+start\+Audio\+Recording (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Audio\+Recording\+Configuration}]{config }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Starts an audio recording.

The S\+DK allows recording during a call, which supports either one of the following formats\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item .wav\+: Large file size with high sound fidelity 
\item .aac\+: Small file size with low sound fidelity 
\end{DoxyItemize}

Ensure that the directory to save the recording file exists and is writable. This method is usually called after the \mbox{\hyperlink{}{token, java.\+lang.\+String channel\+Name, java.\+lang.\+String optional\+Info, int optional\+Uid) join\+Channel}} method. The recording automatically stops when the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_af3fe5d61a9ca8db36b56432273d02307}{leave\+Channel}} method is called.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em config} & audio file recording config \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success. 
\item $<$0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a60a05708b6b2d40b9f3e2bd7aadda143}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a60a05708b6b2d40b9f3e2bd7aadda143}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!stopAudioRecording@{stopAudioRecording}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a5025d9a8b82da0e19a3451e56c40f6c8}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a5025d9a8b82da0e19a3451e56c40f6c8}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!startEchoTest@{startEchoTest}}
\index{startEchoTest@{startEchoTest}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{startEchoTest()}{startEchoTest()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+start\+Echo\+Test (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000030}{Deprecated}}]Now use \mbox{\hyperlink{}{start\+Echo\+Testint}}\end{DoxyRefDesc}


Starts an audio call test to determine whether the audio devices (for example, headset and speaker) and the network connection are working properly.

In the test, the user first speaks, and the recording is played back in 10 seconds. If the user can hear the recording in 10 seconds, it indicates that the audio devices and network connection work properly.

Note\+: After calling the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a5025d9a8b82da0e19a3451e56c40f6c8}{start\+Echo\+Test}} method, call \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_abf712c76582d770457bf8f0b773312fe}{stop\+Echo\+Test}} to end the test; otherwise the application cannot run the next echo test, nor can it call the \mbox{\hyperlink{}{token, java.\+lang.\+String channel\+Name, java.\+lang.\+String optional\+Info, int optional\+Uid) join\+Channel}} method to start a new call.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success. 
\item $<$0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_aa3525887e955b1f2eb14daad674e9e93}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_aa3525887e955b1f2eb14daad674e9e93}}

Starts an audio call test. \begin{DoxySince}{Since}
v2.\+4.\+0. 
\end{DoxySince}
In the audio call test, you record your voice. If the recording plays back within the set time interval, the audio devices and the network connection are working properly.

\item Call this method before joining a channel.

Otherwise, the app cannot run the next echo test, or call the \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a9f46b1374bf38be28d65682b0ea6ade9}{joinchannel\} method.In the {\ttfamily L\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+I\+NG} profile, only a host can call this method.  interval\+In\+Seconds The time interval (s) between when you speak and when the recording plays back. 0\+: Success.$<$ 0\+: Failure. }}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!startLastmileProbeTest@{startLastmileProbeTest}}
\index{startLastmileProbeTest@{startLastmileProbeTest}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{startLastmileProbeTest()}{startLastmileProbeTest()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+start\+Lastmile\+Probe\+Test (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Lastmile\+Probe\+Config}]{config }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Starts the last-\/mile network probe test before joining a channel to get the uplink and downlink last-\/mile network statistics, including the bandwidth, packet loss, jitter, and round-\/trip time (R\+TT).

Once this method is enabled, the S\+DK triggers the \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_adc7bfb05ed741769a1436794926b1cf8}{on\+Lastmile\+Probe\+Result\} callback within 30 seconds, and reports the real-\/time statistics of the network conditions. Call this method to check the uplink network quality before users join a channel or before an audience switches to a host. This method consumes extra network traffic and may affect communication quality.Do not call other methods before receiving the \{ I\+Rtc\+Engine\+Event\+Handler\#on\+Lastmile\+Probe\+Result on\+Lastmile\+Probe\+Result\} callback. Otherwise, the callback may be interrupted by other methods.  config The configurations of the last-\/mile network probe test. For details, see  io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+internal.\+Lastmile\+Probe\+Config Lastmile\+Probe\+Config\}. 0\+: Success.$<$ 0\+: Failure. }}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_ae557f56f8fd4b808bb5c5902d0f1acc5}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_ae557f56f8fd4b808bb5c5902d0f1acc5}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!stopLastmileProbeTest@{stopLastmileProbeTest}}
\index{stopLastmileProbeTest@{stopLastmileProbeTest}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}

\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!pullPlaybackAudioFrame@{pullPlaybackAudioFrame}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{pullPlaybackAudioFrame()}{pullPlaybackAudioFrame()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+pull\+Playback\+Audio\+Frame (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{byte\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]}}]{data,  }\item[{int}]{length\+In\+Byte }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Pulls the remote audio frame.

Before calling this method, call the \mbox{\hyperlink{}{int, int)}} method to enable and set the external audio sink.

Ensure that you call this method after joining a channel.

After a successful method call, the app pulls the decoded and mixed audio data for playback.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em data} & The audio data that you want to pull. The data format is in byte\mbox{[}\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
{\em length\+In\+Byte} & The data length (byte) of the external audio data. The value of this parameter is related to the audio duration, and the values of the {\ttfamily sample\+Rate} and {\ttfamily channels} parameters that you set in \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a63b1e84833597f73666d858208e0d31e}{set\+External\+Audio\+Sink}}. Agora recommends setting the audio duration no shorter than 10 ms. The formula for {\ttfamily length\+In\+Byte} is\+: ~\newline
length\+In\+Byte = sample\+Rate/1000  2  channels  audio duration (ms).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a2daa2138791b3225790d640d009e7b50}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a2daa2138791b3225790d640d009e7b50}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!pullPlaybackAudioFrame@{pullPlaybackAudioFrame}}
\index{pullPlaybackAudioFrame@{pullPlaybackAudioFrame}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{pullPlaybackAudioFrame()}{pullPlaybackAudioFrame()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+pull\+Playback\+Audio\+Frame (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Byte\+Buffer}]{data,  }\item[{int}]{length\+In\+Byte }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Pulls the remote audio frame.

Before calling this method, call the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a63b1e84833597f73666d858208e0d31e}{set\+External\+Audio\+Sink}}(enabled\+: true) method to enable and set the external audio sink.

Ensure that you call this method after joining a channel.

After a successful method call, the app pulls the decoded and mixed audio data for playback.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Once you call the {\ttfamily pull\+Playback\+Audio\+Frame} method successfully, the app will not retrieve any audio data from the \mbox{\hyperlink{}{int, int, int, int, Byte\+Buffer, long, int)}} on\+Playback\+Frame\} callback.
\item The difference between the {\ttfamily on\+Playback\+Frame} callback and the {\ttfamily pull\+Playback\+Audio\+Frame} method is as follows\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily on\+Playback\+Frame}\+: The S\+DK sends the audio data to the app through this callback. Any delay in processing the audio frames may result in audio jitter.
\item {\ttfamily pull\+Playback\+Audio\+Frame}\+: The app pulls the remote audio data. After setting the audio data parameters, the S\+DK adjusts the frame buffer and avoids problems caused by jitter in the external audio playback.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em data} & The audio data that you want to pull. The data format is in Byte\+Buffer. \\
\hline
{\em length\+In\+Byte} & The data length (byte) of the external audio data. The value of this parameter is related to the audio duration, and the values of the {\ttfamily sample\+Rate} and {\ttfamily channels} parameters that you set in \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a63b1e84833597f73666d858208e0d31e}{set\+External\+Audio\+Sink}}. Agora recommends setting the audio duration no shorter than 10 ms. The formula for {\ttfamily length\+In\+Byte} is\+: ~\newline
length\+In\+Byte = sample\+Rate/1000  2  channels  audio duration (ms).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

Starts the microphone test.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+External\+Audio\+Source (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{boolean}]{enabled,  }\item[{int}]{sample\+Rate,  }\item[{int}]{channels }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets the external audio source.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Ensure that you call this method before calling {\ttfamily join\+Channel}.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em enabled} & Determines whether to enable the external audio source\+:

\item true\+: Enable the external audio source.
\item false\+: (default) Disable the external audio source. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em sample\+Rate} & The Sample rate (Hz) of the external audio source, which can set be as 8000, 16000, 32000, 44100, or 48000. \\

{\em channels} & The number of channels of the external audio source, which can be set as 1 or 2\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 1\+: Mono.
\item 2\+: Stereo. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Sets the external audio source.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Ensure that you call this method before {\ttfamily join\+Channel}.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em enabled} & Determines whether to enable the external audio source\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: Enable the external audio source.
\item false\+: (default) Disable the external audio source. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em sample\+Rate} & The Sample rate (Hz) of the external audio source, which can set be as 8000, 16000, 32000, 44100, or 48000. \\
\hline
{\em channels} & The number of channels of the external audio source, which can be set as 1 or 2\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 1\+: Mono.
\item 2\+: Stereo. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em source\+Number} & The number of audio source per channel.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 1\+: Mono.
\item 2\+: Stereo. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\

Sets the external video source.

Once the external video source is enabled, the S\+DK prepares to accept the external video frame.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em enable} & Determines whether to enable the external video source.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: Enable the external video source. Once set, the S\+DK creates the external source and prepares video data from {\ttfamily push\+External\+Video\+Frame} or {\ttfamily push\+External\+Encoded\+Video\+Image}.
\item false\+: Disable the external video source. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em use\+Texture} & Determines whether to use textured video data.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: Use texture, which is not supported now.
\item False\+: Do not use texture. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em source\+Type} & Determines whether the external video source is encoded.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{enumio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_1_1_external_video_source_type}{V\+I\+D\+E\+O\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E(0)}}\+: The external video source is not encoded.
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{enumio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_1_1_external_video_source_type}{E\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+D\+\_\+\+V\+I\+D\+E\+O\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E(1)}}\+: The external video source is encoded. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!pushExternalVideoFrame@{pushExternalVideoFrame}}
\index{pushExternalVideoFrame@{pushExternalVideoFrame}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{pushExternalVideoFrame()}{pushExternalVideoFrame()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract boolean io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+push\+External\+Video\+Frame (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1video_1_1_agora_video_frame}{Agora\+Video\+Frame}}}]{frame }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Pushes the video frame using the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1video_1_1_agora_video_frame}{Agora\+Video\+Frame}} class and passes the video frame to the Agora S\+DK.

Call the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_ac96321fb1017f554bc291a8d08fcefe2}{set\+External\+Video\+Source}} method and set {\ttfamily push\+Mode} as {\ttfamily true} before calling this method. Otherwise, a failure returns after calling this method.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
You can push the video frame either by calling this method or by calling \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a2e84e4ede445e1b024bf3836fae61d26}{push\+External\+Video\+Frame(\+Video\+Frame frame)\}. For textured video frames, Agora recommends using the  push\+External\+Video\+Frame(Video\+Frame frame) push\+External\+Video\+Frame(\+Video\+Frame frame)\} method, so that the S\+DK can better utilize the hardware performance.  frame Video frame to be pushed. See  io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+video.\+Agora\+Video\+Frame Agora\+Video\+Frame\}.  In the {\ttfamily C\+O\+M\+M\+U\+N\+I\+C\+A\+T\+I\+ON} profile, the S\+DK does not support textured video frames. {\ttfamily true}\+: The frame is pushed successfully.{\ttfamily false}\+: Failed to push the frame. }}
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a2e84e4ede445e1b024bf3836fae61d26}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a2e84e4ede445e1b024bf3836fae61d26}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!pushExternalVideoFrame@{pushExternalVideoFrame}}
\index{pushExternalVideoFrame@{pushExternalVideoFrame}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{pushExternalVideoFrame()}{pushExternalVideoFrame()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract boolean io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+push\+External\+Video\+Frame (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1base_1_1_video_frame}{Video\+Frame}}}]{frame }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Pushes the video frame using the {\ttfamily Video\+Frame} class and passes the video frame to the Agora S\+DK.

Call the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_ac96321fb1017f554bc291a8d08fcefe2}{set\+External\+Video\+Source}} method and set {\ttfamily push\+Mode} as {\ttfamily true} before calling this method. Otherwise, a failure returns after calling this method.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
You can push the video frame either by calling this method or by calling \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a139283543acaa618638acd57a9195607}{push\+External\+Video\+Frame(\+Agora\+Video\+Frame frame)\}. For textured video frames, Agora recommends using the  push\+External\+Video\+Frame(Video\+Frame frame) push\+External\+Video\+Frame(\+Video\+Frame frame)\} method, so that the S\+DK can better utilize the hardware performance.  frame Video frame to be pushed. See  Video\+Frame Video\+Frame\}\+:{\ttfamily buffer}\+: {\itshape Buffer} The buffer of the video frame.{\ttfamily rotation}\+: {\itshape int} Rotation of the video frame in degrees.{\ttfamily timestamp\+Ns}\+: {\itshape long} Timestamp of the video frame in nanoseconds.  In the {\ttfamily C\+O\+M\+M\+U\+N\+I\+C\+A\+T\+I\+ON} profile, the S\+DK does not support textured video frames. {\ttfamily true}\+: The frame is pushed successfully.{\ttfamily false}\+: Failed to push the frame. }}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em observer} & The \mbox{\hyperlink{interfaceio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_audio_encoded_frame_observer}{I\+Audio\+Encoded\+Frame\+Observer}} interface, null means unregistering observer instead. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_af4315d888d60b756a9da1ccbfa472032}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_af4315d888d60b756a9da1ccbfa472032}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setRecordingAudioFrameParameters()}{setRecordingAudioFrameParameters()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Recording\+Audio\+Frame\+Parameters (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{sample\+Rate,  }\item[{int}]{channel,  }\item[{int}]{mode,  }\item[{int}]{samples\+Per\+Call }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets the audio recording format for the \mbox{\hyperlink{interfaceio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_audio_frame_observer_a1ee188710b22855bd828a9449fd838d4}{on\+Record\+Audio\+Frame}} callback.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sample\+Rate} & Sets the sample rate ({\ttfamily samples\+Per\+Sec}) returned in the {\ttfamily on\+Record\+Audio\+Frame} callback, which can be set as 8000, 16000, 32000, 44100, or 48000 Hz. \\
\hline
{\em channel} & Sets the number of audio channels (channels) returned in the {\ttfamily on\+Record\+Audio\+Frame} callback\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 1\+: Mono.
\item 2\+: Stereo. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em mode} & Sets the use mode of the on\+Record\+Audio\+Frame callback\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily R\+A\+W\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+O\+P\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+D\+\_\+\+O\+N\+L\+Y(0)}\+: Read-\/only mode\+: Users only read the audio data without modifying anything. For example, when users acquire the data with the Agora S\+DK then push the R\+T\+MP streams.
\item {\ttfamily R\+A\+W\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+O\+P\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+D\+\_\+\+W\+R\+I\+T\+E(2)}\+: Read and write mode\+: Users read the data from Audio\+Frame, modify it, and then play it. For example, when users have their own sound-\/effect processing module and perform some voice pre-\/processing, such as a voice change. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em samples\+Per\+Call} & Sets the number of samples the {\ttfamily on\+Record\+Audio\+Frame} callback returns. In R\+T\+MP streaming scenarios, set it as 1024. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The S\+DK calculates the sample interval according to the value of the {\ttfamily sample\+Rate}, {\ttfamily channel}, and {\ttfamily samples\+Per\+Call} parameters you set in this method. Sample interval (s) = sample\+Per\+Call/(sample\+Rate  channel). Ensure that the value of sample interval $>$= 0.\+01. The S\+DK triggers the {\ttfamily on\+Record\+Audio\+Frame} callback according to the sample interval. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a68b9c77f4879d0c3a9c23b608fb34f0b}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a68b9c77f4879d0c3a9c23b608fb34f0b}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!addVideoWatermark@{addVideoWatermark}}
\index{addVideoWatermark@{addVideoWatermark}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addVideoWatermark()}{addVideoWatermark()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+add\+Video\+Watermark (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1video_1_1_agora_image}{Agora\+Image}}}]{watermark }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Adds a watermark image to the local video.

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000031}{Deprecated}}]From v2.\+9.\+1. We recommend using the \mbox{\hyperlink{}{Watermark\+Options) add\+Video\+Watermark}}2 method instead.\end{DoxyRefDesc}


This method adds a P\+NG watermark image to the local video stream for the sampling device, channel audience, or C\+DN live audience to see and capture. To add the P\+NG file to a C\+DN live publishing stream, see the \mbox{\hyperlink{}{set\+Live\+Transcoding}} method.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em watermark} & Watermark image to be added to the local video stream. See \{\mbox{\hyperlink{}{Agora Image\}.  }} The U\+RL descriptions are different for the local video and C\+DN live streams\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item In a local video stream, {\ttfamily url} in \mbox{\hyperlink{}{Agora Image}} refers to the absolute path of the added watermark image file in the local video stream. 
\item In a C\+DN live stream, {\ttfamily url} in \mbox{\hyperlink{}{Agora Image}} refers to the address of the added watermark image in the C\+DN live streaming. 
\end{DoxyItemize}The source file of the watermark image must be in the P\+NG file format. If the width and height of the P\+NG file differ from your settings in this method, the P\+NG file is cropped to conform to your settings. The Agora S\+DK supports adding only one watermark image onto a local video or C\+DN live stream. The newly added watermark image replaces the previous one. If you set {\ttfamily orientation\+Mode} as Adaptive in the \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a33af5b77701edea3f565e05e2bd7e9d4}{set\+Video\+Encoder\+Configuration\} method, the watermark image rotates with the video frame around the upper left corner of the watermark image. }} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a93cead22d8e71234dce89d55655bac90}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a93cead22d8e71234dce89d55655bac90}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!addVideoWatermark@{addVideoWatermark}}
\index{addVideoWatermark@{addVideoWatermark}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addVideoWatermark()}{addVideoWatermark()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+add\+Video\+Watermark (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{watermark\+Url,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1video_1_1_watermark_options}{Watermark\+Options}}}]{options }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Adds a watermark image to the local video. \begin{DoxySince}{Since}
v2.\+9.\+1 to replace \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a68b9c77f4879d0c3a9c23b608fb34f0b}{add\+Video\+Watermark}}1.
\end{DoxySince}
This method adds a P\+NG watermark image to the local video stream in a live streaming. Once the watermark image is added, all the audience in the channel (C\+DN audience included), and the sampling device can see and capture it.

Agora supports adding only one watermark image onto the local video, and the newly watermark image replaces the previous one.

The watermark position depends on the settings in the \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a33af5b77701edea3f565e05e2bd7e9d4}{set\+Video\+Encoder\+Configuration\} method\+:If the orientation mode of the encoding video is O\+R\+I\+E\+N\+T\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+F\+I\+X\+E\+D\+\_\+\+L\+A\+N\+D\+S\+C\+A\+PE, or the landscape mode in O\+R\+I\+E\+N\+T\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+A\+D\+A\+P\+T\+I\+VE, the watermark uses the landscape orientation.If the orientation mode of the encoding video is O\+R\+I\+E\+N\+T\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+F\+I\+X\+E\+D\+\_\+\+P\+O\+R\+T\+R\+A\+IT, or the portrait mode in O\+R\+I\+E\+N\+T\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+A\+D\+A\+P\+T\+I\+VE, the watermark uses the portrait orientation.When setting the watermark position, the region must be less than the dimensions set in the set\+Video\+Encoder\+Configuration method. Otherwise, the watermark image will be cropped. Ensure that you have called the  Rtc\+Engine\#enable\+Video enable\+Video\} method to enable the video module before calling this method.If you only want to add a watermark image to the local video for the audience in the C\+DN live streaming channel to see and capture, you can call this method or the \{ Rtc\+Engine\#set\+Live\+Transcoding set\+Live\+Transcoding\} method.This method supports adding a watermark image in the P\+NG file format only. Supported pixel formats of the P\+NG image are R\+G\+BA, R\+GB, Palette, Gray, and Alpha\+\_\+gray.If the dimensions the P\+NG image differ from your settings in this method, the image will be cropped or zoomed to conform to your settings.If you have enabled the local video preview by calling the  Rtc\+Engine\#start\+Preview start\+Preview\} method, you can use the {\ttfamily visible\+In\+Preview} member in the {\ttfamily Watermark\+Options} class to set whether or not the watermark is visible in preview.If you have enabled the mirror mode for the local video, the watermark on the local video is also mirrored. To avoid mirroring the watermark, Agora recommends that you do not use the mirror and watermark functions for the local video at the same time. You can implement the watermark function in your application layer.  watermark\+Url The local file path of the watermark image to be added. This method supports adding a watermark image from either the local file path or the assets file path. If you use the assets file path, you need to start with {\ttfamily /assets/} when filling in this parameter.  options The options of the watermark image to be added. See \{ io.\+agora.\+rtc.\+video.\+Watermark\+Options Watermark Options\}. 0\+: Success.$<$ 0\+: Failure. }}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a88d1a9288aea4e51966090d0f5f3d9cf}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a88d1a9288aea4e51966090d0f5f3d9cf}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!clearVideoWatermarks@{clearVideoWatermarks}}
\index{clearVideoWatermarks@{clearVideoWatermarks}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}

\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!setRemoteUserPriority@{setRemoteUserPriority}}
\index{setRemoteUserPriority@{setRemoteUserPriority}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setRemoteUserPriority()}{setRemoteUserPriority()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Remote\+User\+Priority (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{uid,  }\item[{int}]{user\+Priority }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets the priority of a remote user\textquotesingle{}s media stream.

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
v2.\+4.\+0. 
\end{DoxySince}
Use this method with the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a1aa0ca8a4b071602eeca1fca6795e353}{set\+Remote\+Subscribe\+Fallback\+Option}} method. If the fallback function is enabled for a subscribed stream, the S\+DK ensures the high-\/priority user gets the best possible stream quality.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The S\+DK supports setting user\+Priority as high for one user only.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em uid} & The ID of the remote user. \\
\hline
{\em user\+Priority} & The priority of the remote user\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_a76a37ca249bb48c04ab0723016a1cf41}{U\+S\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+R\+I\+O\+R\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H(50)}}\+: the user\textquotesingle{}s priority is high. 
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_ac87dc70bb144efc48cdaaddf1b3c47cf}{U\+S\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+R\+I\+O\+R\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+N\+O\+R\+A\+N\+L(100)}}\+: (default) the user\textquotesingle{}s priority is normal. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success. 
\item $<$0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a036743ea3c7c5850001f5f61ce50b245}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a036743ea3c7c5850001f5f61ce50b245}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!setLocalPublishFallbackOption@{setLocalPublishFallbackOption}}
\index{setLocalPublishFallbackOption@{setLocalPublishFallbackOption}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setLocalPublishFallbackOption()}{setLocalPublishFallbackOption()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Local\+Publish\+Fallback\+Option (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{option }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets the fallback option for the locally published video stream based on the network conditions.

If {\ttfamily option} is set as \mbox{\hyperlink{}{S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+O\+N\+L\+Y(2)}}, the S\+DK will\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Disable the upstream video but enable audio only when the network conditions deteriorate and cannot support both video and audio. 
\item Re-\/enable the video when the network conditions improve. 
\end{DoxyItemize}When the locally published video stream falls back to audio only or when the audio-\/only stream switches back to the video, the S\+DK triggers the \{\mbox{\hyperlink{}{on\+Local\+Publish\+Fallback\+To\+Audio\+Only\}. Ensure that you call this method before joining a channel.  option The fallback option for the locally published video stream\+: io.\+agora.\+rtc.\+Constants\#\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+ED S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+E\+D(0)\}\+: (Default) No fallback behavior for the locally published video stream when the uplink network condition is poor. The stream quality is not guaranteed. io.\+agora.\+rtc.\+Constants\#\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+O\+N\+LY S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+O\+N\+L\+Y(2)\}\+: The locally published video stream falls back to audio only when the uplink network condition is poor.  Agora does not recommend using this method for C\+DN live streaming, because the remote C\+DN live user will have a noticeable lag when the locally published video stream falls back to audio only. 0\+: Success.$<$ 0\+: Failure. }}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a1aa0ca8a4b071602eeca1fca6795e353}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a1aa0ca8a4b071602eeca1fca6795e353}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!setRemoteSubscribeFallbackOption@{setRemoteSubscribeFallbackOption}}
\index{setRemoteSubscribeFallbackOption@{setRemoteSubscribeFallbackOption}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setRemoteSubscribeFallbackOption()}{setRemoteSubscribeFallbackOption()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Remote\+Subscribe\+Fallback\+Option (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{option }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets the fallback option for the remotely subscribed video stream based on the network conditions.

If {\ttfamily option} is set as \mbox{\hyperlink{}{S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+O\+N\+L\+Y(2)}}, the S\+DK automatically switches the video from a high-\/stream to a low-\/stream, or disables the video when the downlink network condition cannot support both audio and video to guarantee the quality of the audio. The S\+DK monitors the network quality and restores the video stream when the network conditions improve. When the remotely subscribed video stream falls back to audio only, or the audio-\/only stream switches back to the video, the S\+DK triggers the \{\mbox{\hyperlink{}{on\+Remote\+Subscribe\+Fallback\+To\+Audio\+Only\} callback. Ensure that you call this method before joining a channel.  option The fallback option for the remotely subscribed video stream\+: io.\+agora.\+rtc.\+Constants\#\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+ED S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+E\+D(0)\}\+: No fallback behavior for the remotely subscribed video stream when the downlink network condition is poor. The quality of the video stream is not guaranteed. io.\+agora.\+rtc.\+Constants\#\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+V\+I\+D\+E\+O\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+L\+OW S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+V\+I\+D\+E\+O\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+L\+O\+W(1)\}\+: (Default) The remotely subscribed video stream falls back to the low-\/stream video when the downlink network condition worsens. This option works only for this method and not for the \{ io.\+agora.\+rtc.\+Rtc\+Engine\#set\+Local\+Publish\+Fallback\+Option(int) set\+Local\+Publish\+Fallback\+Option\} method. io.\+agora.\+rtc.\+Constants\#\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+O\+N\+LY S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+O\+N\+L\+Y(2)\}\+: Under poor downlink network conditions, the remotely subscribed video stream first falls back to the low-\/stream video; and then to an audio-\/only stream if the network condition worsens. 0\+: Success.$<$ 0\+: Failure. }}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_ab409b3e574bee1ee8187bf2540236b66}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_ab409b3e574bee1ee8187bf2540236b66}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enableDualStreamMode()}{enableDualStreamMode()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+enable\+Dual\+Stream\+Mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{boolean}]{enabled }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Enables or disables the dual video stream mode.

If dual-\/stream mode is enabled, the subscriber can choose to receive the high-\/stream (high-\/resolution high-\/bitrate video stream) or low-\/stream (low-\/resolution low-\/bitrate video stream) video using \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a56c63259b129c1beeb0ee121b353fc2f}{set\+Remote\+Video\+Stream\+Type}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em enabled} & 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: Enable the dual-\/stream mode.
\item false\+: (default) Disable the dual-\/stream mode. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_aea4bf3f92298a40c7b83be2fe3e52144}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_aea4bf3f92298a40c7b83be2fe3e52144}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setRemoteVideoStreamType()}{setRemoteVideoStreamType()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Remote\+Video\+Stream\+Type (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{uid,  }\item[{int}]{stream\+Type }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets the remote video stream type.

If the remote user has enabled the dual-\/stream mode, by default the S\+DK receives the high-\/stream video by Call this method to switch to the low-\/stream video.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This method applies to scenarios where the remote user has enabled the dual-\/stream mode using \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_ab409b3e574bee1ee8187bf2540236b66}{enable\+Dual\+Stream\+Mode}}(true) before joining the channel.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em uid} & ID of the remote user sending the video stream. \\
\hline
{\em stream\+Type} & Sets the video stream type\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: High-\/stream video.
\item 1\+: Low-\/stream video.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyNote}

\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!setEncryptionSecret@{setEncryptionSecret}}
\index{setEncryptionSecret@{setEncryptionSecret}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setEncryptionSecret()}{setEncryptionSecret()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Encryption\+Secret (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{secret }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Specifies an encryption password to enable built-\/in encryption before joining a channel.

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000032}{Deprecated}}]This method is deprecated.\end{DoxyRefDesc}


All users in a channel must set the same encryption password. The encryption password is automatically cleared once a user has left the channel. If the encryption password is not specified or set to empty, the encryption function will be disabled.

Note\+: Do not use this function together with C\+DN.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em secret} & Encryption Password \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success. 
\item $<$0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setEncryptionMode()}{setEncryptionMode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Encryption\+Mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{encryption\+Mode }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets the built-\/in encryption mode.

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000033}{Deprecated}}]This method is deprecated.\end{DoxyRefDesc}


The Agora Native S\+DK supports built-\/in encryption. Call this A\+PI to set the encryption mode. 

All users in the same channel must use the same encryption mode and password. Refer to information related to the encryption algorithm on the differences between encryption modes. 

Call \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a80f3483745062772033c0b6b7aba724a}{set\+Encryption\+Secret}} to enable the built-\/in encryption function before calling this A\+PI.

Note\+: Do not use this function together with C\+DN.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em encryption\+Mode} & Encryption mode\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \char`\"{}sm4-\/128-\/ecb\char`\"{}\+: 128-\/bit S\+M4 encryption, E\+CB mode 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success. 
\item $<$0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a840d57b187d64b8903078a6dcc879c67}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a840d57b187d64b8903078a6dcc879c67}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!enableEncryption@{enableEncryption}}
\index{enableEncryption@{enableEncryption}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enableEncryption()}{enableEncryption()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+enable\+Encryption (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{boolean}]{enabled,  }\item[{Encryption\+Config}]{config }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Enables/\+Disables the built-\/in encryption.

In scenarios requiring high security, Agora recommends calling {\ttfamily enable\+Encryption} to enable the built-\/in encryption before joining a channel.

All users in the same channel must use the same encryption mode and encryption key. Once all users leave the channel, the encryption key of this channel is automatically cleared.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If you enable the built-\/in encryption, you cannot use the R\+T\+MP streaming function. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em enabled} & Whether to enable the built-\/in encryption.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily true}\+: Enable the built-\/in encryption.
\item {\ttfamily false}\+: Disable the built-\/in encryption. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em config} & Configurations of built-\/in encryption schemas. See \{\mbox{\hyperlink{}{Encryption\+Config\}. 0\+: Success.$<$ 0\+: Failure.-\/2(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+R\+G\+U\+M\+E\+NT)\+: An invalid parameter is used. Set the parameter with a valid value.-\/7(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+I\+N\+I\+T\+I\+A\+L\+I\+Z\+E\+D\+: The S\+DK is not initialized. Initialize the I\+Rtc\+Engine instance before calling this method.-\/4(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+ED)\+: The encryption mode is incorrect or the S\+DK fails to load the external encryption library. Check the enumeration or reload the external encryption library. }}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a61e6a515d2c687ae3879e46c804073f4}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a61e6a515d2c687ae3879e46c804073f4}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!startRtmpStreamWithoutTranscoding@{startRtmpStreamWithoutTranscoding}}
\index{startRtmpStreamWithoutTranscoding@{startRtmpStreamWithoutTranscoding}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{startRtmpStreamWithoutTranscoding()}{startRtmpStreamWithoutTranscoding()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+start\+Rtmp\+Stream\+Without\+Transcoding (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{url }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Publishes the local stream without transcoding to a specified C\+DN live R\+T\+MP address. (C\+DN live only.)

The S\+DK returns the result of this method call in the on\+Stream\+Published callback.

The start\+Rtmp\+Stream\+Without\+Transcoding method call triggers the on\+Rtmp\+Streaming\+State\+Changed callback on the local client to report the state of adding a local stream to the C\+DN. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Ensure that the user joins the channel before calling this method.
\item This method adds only one stream R\+T\+MP U\+RL address each time it is called.
\item The R\+T\+MP U\+RL address must not contain special characters, such as Chinese language characters.
\item This method applies to Live Broadcast only.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em url} & The C\+DN streaming U\+RL in the R\+T\+MP format. The maximum length of this parameter is 1024 bytes.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \#\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+R\+G\+U\+M\+E\+NT (2)\+: The R\+T\+MP U\+RL address is N\+U\+LL or has a string length of 0.
\item \#\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+I\+N\+I\+T\+I\+A\+L\+I\+Z\+ED (7)\+: You have not initialized the R\+TC engine when publishing the stream. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a556d466c4b0ee61888bb459810c8ded8}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a556d466c4b0ee61888bb459810c8ded8}}

The S\+DK returns the result of this method call in the on\+Stream\+Published callback.

The start\+Rtmp\+Stream\+With\+Transcoding method call triggers the on\+Rtmp\+Streaming\+State\+Changed callback on the local client to report the state of adding a local stream to the C\+DN. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Ensure that the user joins the channel before calling this method.
\item This method adds only one stream R\+T\+MP U\+RL address each time it is called.
\item The R\+T\+MP U\+RL address must not contain special characters, such as Chinese language characters.
\item This method applies to Live Broadcast only.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: Enable transcoding. To \href{https://docs.agora.io/en/Agora\%20Platform/terms?platform=All\%20Platforms\#transcoding}{\texttt{ transcode}} the audio or video streams when publishing them to C\+DN live, often used for combining the audio and video streams of multiple hosts in C\+DN live.
\item false\+: Disable transcoding.

\item \#\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+I\+N\+I\+T\+I\+A\+L\+I\+Z\+ED (7)\+: You have not initialized the R\+TC engine when publishing the stream.

\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!stopRtmpStream@{stopRtmpStream}}
\index{stopRtmpStream@{stopRtmpStream}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{stopRtmpStream()}{stopRtmpStream()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+stop\+Rtmp\+Stream (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{url }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Stop an R\+T\+MP stream with transcoding or without transcoding from the C\+DN. (C\+DN live only.)

This method removes the R\+T\+MP U\+RL address (added by the start\+Rtmp\+Stream\+Without\+Transcoding method or I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::start\+Rtmp\+Stream\+With\+Transcoding \char`\"{}start\+Rtmp\+Stream\+With\+Transcoding\char`\"{} method) from a C\+DN live stream. The S\+DK returns the result of this method call in the on\+Stream\+Unpublished callback.

The stop\+Rtmp\+Stream method call triggers the on\+Rtmp\+Streaming\+State\+Changed callback on the local client to report the state of removing an R\+T\+MP stream from the C\+DN. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This method removes only one R\+T\+MP U\+RL address each time it is called.
\item The R\+T\+MP U\+RL address must not contain special characters, such as Chinese language characters.
\item This method applies to Live Broadcast only.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em url} & The R\+T\+MP U\+RL address to be removed. The maximum length of this parameter is 1024 bytes.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a39490ffa0d4312521e6b81c10e9ae03c}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a39490ffa0d4312521e6b81c10e9ae03c}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!createDataStream@{createDataStream}}
\index{createDataStream@{createDataStream}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{createDataStream()}{createDataStream()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+create\+Data\+Stream (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{boolean}]{reliable,  }\item[{boolean}]{ordered }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Creates a data stream.

You can call this method to create a data stream and improve the reliability and ordering of data transmission.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Ensure that you set the same value for {\ttfamily reliable} and {\ttfamily ordered}.
\item Each user can only create a maximum of 5 data streams during an \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}} lifecycle.
\item The data channel allows a data delay of up to 5 seconds. If the receiver does not receive the data stream within 5 seconds, the data channel reports an error.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em reliable} & Sets whether the recipients are guaranteed to receive the data stream from the sender within five seconds\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: The recipients receive the data stream from the sender within five seconds. If the recipient does not receive the data stream within five seconds, an error is reported to the application.
\item false\+: There is no guarantee that the recipients receive the data stream within five seconds and no error message is reported for any delay or missing data stream. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em ordered} & Sets whether the recipients receive the data stream in the sent order\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: The recipients receive the data stream in the sent order.
\item false\+: The recipients do not receive the data stream in the sent order. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Returns the stream ID, if the method call is successful.
\item $<$0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a32f33f1ffad6dac643490c2c6fdf938f}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a32f33f1ffad6dac643490c2c6fdf938f}}

Creates a data stream.

Each user can create up to five data streams during the lifecycle of the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine}{Rtc\+Engine}}.

For example, if it returns -\/2, then it indicates  Constants\#\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+R\+G\+U\+M\+E\+NT E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+R\+G\+U\+M\+E\+NT(-\/2)\} in \{ I\+Rtc\+Engine\+Event\+Handler\#on\+Error(int) Error Codes\}. }}
