\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a08e5c46d5b2eaf8fa96f43f7bb4002c8}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a08e5c46d5b2eaf8fa96f43f7bb4002c8}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!sendStreamMessage@{sendStreamMessage}}
\index{sendStreamMessage@{sendStreamMessage}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{sendStreamMessage()}{sendStreamMessage()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+send\+Stream\+Message (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{stream\+Id,  }\item[{byte\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]}}]{message }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sends a data stream.

After calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a39490ffa0d4312521e6b81c10e9ae03c}{~create\+Data\+Stream}}, you can call this method to send a data stream to all users in the channel.

The S\+DK has the following restrictions on this method\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Up to 60 packets can be sent per second in a channel with each packet having a maximum size of 1 KB.
\item Each client can send up to 30 KB of data per second.
\item Each user can have up to five data streams simultaneously.
\end{DoxyItemize}

After the remote user receives the data stream within 5 seconds, the S\+DK triggers the \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a6f827b82ff6ed61e855bf6315aa4395c}{on\+Stream\+Message\} callback on the remote client. After the remote user does not receive the data stream within 5 seconds, the S\+DK triggers the \{ I\+Rtc\+Engine\+Event\+Handler\#on\+Stream\+Message\+Error() on\+Stream\+Message\+Error\} callback. Call this method after calling  Rtc\+Engine\#create\+Data\+Stream()~create\+Data\+Stream\}.This method applies only to the {\ttfamily C\+O\+M\+M\+U\+N\+I\+C\+A\+T\+I\+ON} profile or to the hosts in the {\ttfamily L\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+I\+NG} profile. If an audience in the {\ttfamily L\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+I\+NG} profile calls this method, the audience may be switched to a host.  stream\+Id ID of the sent data stream returned by the \{ Rtc\+Engine\#create\+Data\+Stream(boolean reliable, boolean ordered) create\+Data\+Stream\} method.  message Sent data. 0\+: Success.$<$ 0\+: Failure. }}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_adc13362ddd02df1d4215b97d3c65a4da}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_adc13362ddd02df1d4215b97d3c65a4da}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Local\+Video\+Mirror\+Mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{mode }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets the local video mirror mode.

Use this method before calling the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a316bdab24f10e892955571788bbaccc2}{start\+Preview}} method, or the mirror mode does not take effect until you call the {\ttfamily start\+Preview} method again. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mirror\+Mode} & Sets the local video mirror mode\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily V\+I\+D\+E\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+A\+U\+T\+O(0)}\+: (Default) The mirror mode determined by the S\+DK. If you use the front camera, the S\+DK enables the mirror mode; if you use the rear camera, the S\+DK disables the mirror mode.
\item {\ttfamily V\+I\+D\+E\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+D(1)}\+: Enable the mirror mode.
\item {\ttfamily V\+I\+D\+E\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+E\+D(2)}\+: Disable the mirror mode.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a8878aa59bdf6e8f328ebadf32ec40273}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a8878aa59bdf6e8f328ebadf32ec40273}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!getCallId@{getCallId}}
\index{getCallId@{getCallId}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getCallId()}{getCallId()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract String io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+get\+Call\+Id (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Gets the current call ID.

When a user joins a channel on a client, a {\ttfamily call\+Id} is generated to identify the call.

After a call ends, you can call {\ttfamily rate} or {\ttfamily complain} to gather feedback from the customer. These methods require a {\ttfamily call\+Id} parameter. To use these feedback methods, call the this method first to retrieve the {\ttfamily call\+Id} during the call, and then pass the value as an argument in the {\ttfamily rate} or {\ttfamily complain} method after the call ends.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The call ID if the method call is successful.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_afb97d530cdc8295043ab074d89d5f54c}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_afb97d530cdc8295043ab074d89d5f54c}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!rate@{rate}}
\index{rate@{rate}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{rate()}{rate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+rate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{call\+Id,  }\item[{int}]{rating,  }\item[{String}]{description }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Allows a user to rate the call.

It is usually called after the call ends.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em call\+Id} & The call ID retrieved from the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a8878aa59bdf6e8f328ebadf32ec40273}{get\+Call\+Id}} method. \\
\hline
{\em rating} & The rating of the call between 1 (the lowest score) to 5 (the highest score). \\
\hline
{\em description} & (Optional) The description of the rating. The string length must be less than 800 bytes.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

Allows a user to complain about the call quality.

\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!setLogFile@{setLogFile}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setLogFile()}{setLogFile()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Log\+File (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{file\+Path }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Specifies an S\+DK output log file.

The log file records all log data for the S\+D\+Ks operation. Ensure that the directory for the log file exists and is writable.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Ensure that you call this method immediately after \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a30d9a5c1a0e0500e8f5b94c2063450d5}{create}}, or the output log may not be complete.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em file\+Path} & File path of the log file. The string of the log file is in U\+T\+F-\/8.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_abdab41e7cb1d8c8549ca7db248a78216}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_abdab41e7cb1d8c8549ca7db248a78216}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!setLogFilter@{setLogFilter}}
\index{setLogFilter@{setLogFilter}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setLogFilter()}{setLogFilter()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Log\+Filter (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{filter }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets the output log filter level of the S\+DK.

You can use one or a combination of the filters. The log level follows the sequence of {\ttfamily O\+FF}, {\ttfamily C\+R\+I\+T\+I\+C\+AL}, {\ttfamily E\+R\+R\+OR}, {\ttfamily W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG}, {\ttfamily I\+N\+FO}, and {\ttfamily D\+E\+B\+UG}. Choose a level and you will see logs preceding that level. For example, if you set the log level to {\ttfamily W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG}, you see the logs within levels {\ttfamily C\+R\+I\+T\+I\+C\+AL}, {\ttfamily E\+R\+R\+OR}, and {\ttfamily W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em filter} & Sets the log filter level\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily L\+O\+G\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+D\+E\+B\+U\+G(0x80f)}\+: Output all A\+PI logs. Set your log filter as D\+E\+B\+UG if you want to get the most complete log file.
\item {\ttfamily L\+O\+G\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+F\+O(0x0f)}\+: Output logs of the C\+R\+I\+T\+I\+C\+AL, E\+R\+R\+OR, W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG, and I\+N\+FO level. We recommend setting your log filter as this level.
\item {\ttfamily L\+O\+G\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+N\+G(0x0e)}\+: Output logs of the C\+R\+I\+T\+I\+C\+AL, E\+R\+R\+OR, and W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG level.
\item {\ttfamily L\+O\+G\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R(0x0c)}\+: Output logs of the C\+R\+I\+T\+I\+C\+AL and E\+R\+R\+OR level.
\item {\ttfamily L\+O\+G\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+C\+R\+I\+T\+I\+C\+A\+L(0x08)}\+: Output logs of the C\+R\+I\+T\+I\+C\+AL level.
\item {\ttfamily L\+O\+G\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+O\+F\+F(0)}\+: Do not output any log.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a55e1c586d3885c4f0d43aecfbd3729f2}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a55e1c586d3885c4f0d43aecfbd3729f2}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setLogFileSize()}{setLogFileSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Log\+File\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{long}]{file\+Size\+In\+K\+Bytes }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets the log file size (KB).

The S\+DK has two log files, each with a default size of 512 KB. If you set {\ttfamily file\+Size\+In\+Bytes} as 1024 KB, the S\+DK outputs log files with a total maximum size of 2 MB. If the total size of the log files exceed the set value, the new output log files overwrite the old output log files.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em file\+Size\+In\+K\+Bytes} & The S\+DK log file size (KB). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+register\+Media\+Metadata\+Observer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{interfaceio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_metadata_observer}{I\+Metadata\+Observer}}}]{observer,  }\item[{int}]{type }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Registers the metadata observer.

You need to implement the \mbox{\hyperlink{interfaceio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_metadata_observer}{I\+Metadata\+Observer}} class and specify the metadata type in this method. This method enables you to add synchronized metadata in the video stream for more diversified live interactive streaming, such as sending shopping links, digital coupons, and online quizzes.

A successful call of this method triggers the \{\mbox{\hyperlink{interfaceio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_metadata_observer_a7c56f037df6e7076e32391b32e6e46cd}{get\+Max\+Metadata\+Size\} callback. Call this method before the {\ttfamily join\+Channel} method.This method applies to the Live Broadcast profile.  observer The I\+Metadata\+Observer class.  type The metadata type. Currently, the S\+DK supports \{ io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+I\+Metadata\+Observer\#\+V\+I\+D\+E\+O\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+TA V\+I\+D\+E\+O\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+T\+A(0)\} only. io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+I\+Metadata\+Observer\#\+U\+N\+K\+N\+O\+W\+N\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+TA U\+N\+K\+N\+O\+W\+N\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+TA(-\/1)\}\+: the metadata type is unknown. io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+I\+Metadata\+Observer\#\+V\+I\+D\+E\+O\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+TA V\+I\+D\+E\+O\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+T\+A(0)\}\+: the metadata type is video. 0\+: Success.$<$ 0\+: Failure. }}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a526ccf46b52f43deb9a37c88abbbac04}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a526ccf46b52f43deb9a37c88abbbac04}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+start\+Channel\+Media\+Relay (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1video_1_1_channel_media_relay_configuration}{Channel\+Media\+Relay\+Configuration}}}]{channel\+Media\+Relay\+Configuration }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Starts to relay media streams across channels.

After a successful method call, the S\+DK triggers the \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a3d4f978004d0666f26345810dcfe73ac}{on\+Channel\+Media\+Relay\+State\+Changed\} and  I\+Rtc\+Engine\+Event\+Handler\#on\+Channel\+Media\+Relay\+Event on\+Channel\+Media\+Relay\+Event\} callbacks, and these callbacks return the state and events of the media stream relay.If the {\ttfamily on\+Channel\+Media\+Relay\+State\+Changed} callback returns {\ttfamily R\+E\+L\+A\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+U\+N\+N\+I\+N\+G(2)} and {\ttfamily R\+E\+L\+A\+Y\+\_\+\+O\+K(0)}, and the {\ttfamily on\+Channel\+Media\+Relay\+Event} callback returns {\ttfamily R\+E\+L\+A\+Y\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+P\+A\+C\+K\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+T\+O\+\_\+\+D\+E\+S\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+A\+N\+N\+E\+L(4)}, the S\+DK starts relaying media streams between the original and the destination channel.If the {\ttfamily on\+Channel\+Media\+Relay\+State\+Changed} callback returns {\ttfamily R\+E\+L\+A\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+R\+E(3)}, an exception occurs during the media stream relay. Contact \href{mailto:sales-us@agora.io}{\texttt{ sales-\/us@agora.\+io}} before implementing this function.We do not support string user accounts in this A\+PI.Call this method after the {\ttfamily join\+Channel} method.This method takes effect only when you are a broadcaster in a Live-\/broadcast channel.After a successful method call, if you want to call this method again, ensure that you call the  stop\+Channel\+Media\+Relay stop\+Channel\+Media\+Relay\} method to quit the current relay.  channel\+Media\+Relay\+Configuration The configuration of the media stream relay. See \{ io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+video.\+Channel\+Media\+Relay\+Configuration Channel\+Media\+Relay\+Configuration\}. 0\+: Success.$<$ 0\+: Failure. }}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a4f7f548ec0a720db0e83314755dc5015}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a4f7f548ec0a720db0e83314755dc5015}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!stopChannelMediaRelay@{stopChannelMediaRelay}}
\index{stopChannelMediaRelay@{stopChannelMediaRelay}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{stopChannelMediaRelay()}{stopChannelMediaRelay()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+stop\+Channel\+Media\+Relay (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Stops the media stream relay.

Once the relay stops, the broadcaster quits all the destination channels. After a successful method call, the S\+DK triggers the \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a3d4f978004d0666f26345810dcfe73ac}{on\+Channel\+Media\+Relay\+State\+Changed\} callback. If the callback returns {\ttfamily R\+E\+L\+A\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+I\+D\+L\+E(0)} and {\ttfamily R\+E\+L\+A\+Y\+\_\+\+O\+K(0)}, the broadcaster successfully stops the relay.  If the method call fails, the S\+DK triggers the {\ttfamily on\+Channel\+Media\+Relay\+State\+Changed} callback with the {\ttfamily R\+E\+L\+A\+Y\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+\+S\+E\+R\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+N\+O\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+P\+O\+N\+S\+E(2)} or {\ttfamily R\+E\+L\+A\+Y\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+\+S\+E\+R\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+L\+O\+S\+T(8)} state code. You can leave the channel by calling the  leave\+Channel() leave\+Channel\} method, and the media stream relay automatically stops. 0\+: Success.$<$ 0\+: Failure. }}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a725f9a9cf270b8a32ad5e8c964598219}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a725f9a9cf270b8a32ad5e8c964598219}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Playback\+Audio\+Frame\+Before\+Mixing\+Parameters (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{sample\+Rate,  }\item[{int}]{channel }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets the audio playback format before mixing for the \mbox{\hyperlink{interfaceio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_audio_frame_observer_a4b71855b33cd6f3c9d128a2c7eea2b06}{on\+Playback\+Audio\+Frame\+Before\+Mixing}} callback.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sample\+Rate} & Sets the sample rate ({\ttfamily samples\+Per\+Sec}) returned in the {\ttfamily on\+Playback\+Audio\+Frame\+Before\+Mixing} callback, which can be set as 8000, 16000, 32000, 44100, or 48000 Hz. \\
\hline
{\em channel} & Number of channels of the audio data returned in {\ttfamily on\+Playback\+Audio\+Frame\+Before\+Mixing}, which can be set as 1 or 2\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 1\+: Mono
\item 2\+: Stereo 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The S\+DK calculates the sample interval according to the value of the {\ttfamily sample\+Rate} and {\ttfamily channel} parameters you set in this method. Ensure that the value of sample interval $>$= 0.\+01. The S\+DK triggers the {\ttfamily on\+Playback\+Audio\+Frame\+Before\+Mixing} callback according to the sample interval. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_abbe5abac7982c43a2333e7af804d387d}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_abbe5abac7982c43a2333e7af804d387d}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!preloadEffect@{preloadEffect}}
\index{preloadEffect@{preloadEffect}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{preloadEffect()}{preloadEffect()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+preload\+Effect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{sound\+Id,  }\item[{String}]{file\+Path }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Preloads a specified audio effect.

This method preloads only one specified audio effect into the memory each time it is called. To preload multiple audio effects, call this method multiple times.

After preloading, you can call \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a890999cd19b7dbebececfbb2537637d8}{~play\+Effect}} to play the preloaded audio effect or call \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a3fdc448786337757f696ecdad4f2fcf1}{~play\+All\+Effects}} to play all the preloaded audio effects.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item To ensure smooth communication, limit the size of the audio effect file.
\item Agora recommends calling this method before joining the channel.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sound\+Id} & The ID of the audio effect. \\
\hline
{\em file\+Path} & The absolute path of the local audio effect file or the U\+RL of the online audio effect file. Supported audio formats\+: mp3, mp4, m4a, aac, 3gp, mkv and wav.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_adfec464b6a60ecb5f071df5c44e44954}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_adfec464b6a60ecb5f071df5c44e44954}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!preloadEffect@{preloadEffect}}
\index{preloadEffect@{preloadEffect}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{preloadEffect()}{preloadEffect()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+preload\+Effect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{sound\+Id,  }\item[{String}]{file\+Path,  }\item[{int}]{start\+Pos }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Preloads a specified audio effect.

This method preloads only one specified audio effect into the memory each time it is called. To preload multiple audio effects, call this method multiple times.

After preloading, you can call \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a890999cd19b7dbebececfbb2537637d8}{~play\+Effect}} to play the preloaded audio effect or call \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a3fdc448786337757f696ecdad4f2fcf1}{~play\+All\+Effects}} to play all the preloaded audio effects.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item To ensure smooth communication, limit the size of the audio effect file.
\item Agora recommends calling this method before joining the channel.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sound\+Id} & The ID of the audio effect. \\
\hline
{\em file\+Path} & The absolute path of the local audio effect file or the U\+RL \\
\hline
{\em start\+Pos} & The start position of the online audio effect file. Supported audio formats\+: mp3, mp4, m4a, aac, 3gp, mkv and wav.\\

\end{DoxyParams}

\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!playEffect@{playEffect}}
\index{playEffect@{playEffect}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{playEffect()}{playEffect()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+play\+Effect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{sound\+Id,  }\item[{String}]{file\+Path,  }\item[{int}]{loop\+Count,  }\item[{double}]{pitch,  }\item[{double}]{pan,  }\item[{double}]{gain,  }\item[{boolean}]{publish }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Plays a specified audio effect.

After calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_abbe5abac7982c43a2333e7af804d387d}{preload\+Effect}}, you can call this method to play the specified audio effect for all users in the channel.

This method plays only one specified audio effect each time it is called. To play multiple audio effects, call this method multiple times.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Agora recommends playing no more than three audio effects at the same time.
\item The ID and file path of the audio effect in this method must be the same as that in the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_abbe5abac7982c43a2333e7af804d387d}{preload\+Effect}} method.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sound\+Id} & The ID of the audio effect. \\
\hline
{\em file\+Path} & The absolute path of the local audio effect file or the U\+RL of the online audio effect file. Supported audio formats\+: mp3, mp4, m4a, aac, 3gp, mkv and wav. \\
\hline
{\em loop\+Count} & The number of times the audio effect loops\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily -\/1}\+: Play the audio effect in an indefinite loop until you call \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a4835e9cae6ab8ee92d28384b034e27e5}{stop\+Effect\} or  Rtc\+Engine\#stop\+All\+Effects() stop\+All\+Effects\}.{\ttfamily 0}\+: Play the audio effect once.{\ttfamily 1}\+: Play the audio effect twice.  pitch The pitch of the audio effect. The value ranges between 0.\+5 and 2.\+0. The default value is 1.\+0 (original pitch). The lower the value, the lower the pitch.  pan The spatial position of the audio effect. The value ranges between -\/1.\+0 and 1.\+0\+:{\ttfamily -\/1.\+0}\+: The audio effect shows on the left.{\ttfamily 0.\+0}\+: The audio effect shows ahead.{\ttfamily 1.\+0}\+: The audio effect shows on the right.  gain The volume of the audio effect. The value ranges between 0.\+0 and 100.\+0. The default value is 100 (original volume). The lower the value, the lower the volume of the audio effect.  publish Sets whether to publish the specified audio effect to the remote stream\+:True\+: Publish the audio effect to the remote.False\+: false\+: Do not publish the audio effect to the remote. 0\+: Success.$<$ 0\+: Failure. }}
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_afae7503ed2b7e1ec963f98774d0d0e16}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_afae7503ed2b7e1ec963f98774d0d0e16}}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Agora recommends playing no more than three audio effects at the same time.
\item The ID and file path of the audio effect in this method must be the same as that in the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_abbe5abac7982c43a2333e7af804d387d}{preload\+Effect}} method.

The value ranges between 0.\+0 and 100.\+0. The default value is {\ttfamily 100} (original volume). The lower the value, the lower the volume of the audio effect.  publish Sets whether to publish the specified audio effect to the remote stream\+:True\+: Publish the audio effect to the remote.False\+: Do not publish the audio effect to the remote. 0\+: Success.$<$ 0\+: Failure. }}

Gets the duration of the audio effect file.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Call this method after joining a channel.
\item For the audio file formats supported by this method, see \href{https://docs.agora.io/en/faq/audio_format}{\texttt{ What formats of audio files does the Agora R\+TC S\+DK support}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em file\+Path} & The file path of a local file, including the filename extensions. Agora supports using a U\+RI address, an absolute path, or a path that starts with /assets/. {\bfseries{Note}}\+: You might encounter permission issues if you use an absolute path to access a local file, so Agora recommends using a U\+RI address instead. For example\+: \char`\"{}content\+://com.\+android.\+providers.\+media.\+documents/document/audio\%3\+A14441\char`\"{}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {$\ge$} 0\+: A successful method call. Returns the total duration (ms) of the specified audio effect file.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}!startScreenCapture@{startScreenCapture}}
\index{startScreenCapture@{startScreenCapture}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{startScreenCapture()}{startScreenCapture()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+start\+Screen\+Capture (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_screen_capture_parameters}{Screen\+Capture\+Parameters}}}]{screen\+Capture\+Parameters }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Starts screen sharing.

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
v3.\+7.\+0
\end{DoxySince}
During screen sharing, make sure the user has granted screen capture permission to the application and the Android A\+PI level is not earlier than 21; otherwise, the S\+DK reports error codes \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_af0814cbea65fa2f4cece1c0b94db7fc3}{E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+C\+R\+E\+E\+N\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+T\+U\+R\+E\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+M\+I\+S\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+D\+E\+N\+I\+E\+D(16)}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_a391b7241b8f5e30396337aa09ed116b1}{E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+C\+R\+E\+E\+N\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+T\+U\+R\+E\+\_\+\+S\+Y\+S\+T\+E\+M\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+E\+D(2)}}. To capture system audio during screen sharing, ensure that the Android A\+PI level is not earlier than 29 as well; otherwise, the S\+DK reports the error code \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_af1e60ae87c55b48983e0f6f6ba0c12ec}{E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+C\+R\+E\+E\+N\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+T\+U\+R\+E\+\_\+\+S\+Y\+S\+T\+E\+M\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+E\+D(3)}}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Call this method after joining a channel.
\item On Android 9 and later, to avoid the application being killed by the system after going to the background, Agora recommends you add the foreground service permission ({\ttfamily android.\+permission.\+F\+O\+R\+E\+G\+R\+O\+U\+N\+D\+\_\+\+S\+E\+R\+V\+I\+CE}) to the {\ttfamily /app/\+Manifests/\+Android\+Manifest.xml} file.
\item The billing of the screen sharing stream is based on the values of width and height in {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_screen_capture_parameters}{Screen\+Capture\+Parameters}}}. When you do not pass in these value, Agora bills you at 1280  720; when you pass in these values, Agora bills you at those value. For details, see \href{https://docs.agora.io/en/Interactive\%20Broadcast/billing_rtc}{\texttt{ Pricing for Real-\/time Communication}}.
\item Due to performance limitations, screen sharing is not supported on Android TV.
\item Due to system limitations, if you are using Huawei phones, do not adjust the video encoding resolution of the screen sharing stream during the screen sharing, or you could experience crashes.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em screen\+Capture\+Parameters} & The configuration of the screen sharing. See \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_screen_capture_parameters}{Screen\+Capture\+Parameters\}. 0\+: Success.$<$ 0\+: Failure. }}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_aaa8a6ef8909cebd023c5c229d35fb472}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_aaa8a6ef8909cebd023c5c229d35fb472}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{registerVideoFrameObserver()}{registerVideoFrameObserver()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+register\+Video\+Frame\+Observer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{interfaceio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1video_1_1_i_video_frame_observer}{I\+Video\+Frame\+Observer}}}]{observer }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Registers a video frame observer object.

You need to implement the \mbox{\hyperlink{interfaceio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1video_1_1_i_video_frame_observer}{I\+Video\+Frame\+Observer}} class in this method, and register callbacks according to your scenarios.

After you successfully register the video frame observer, the S\+DK triggers the registered callbacks each time a video frame is received.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
When handling the video data returned in the callbacks, pay attention to the changes in the {\ttfamily width} and {\ttfamily height} parameters, which may be adapted under the following circumstances\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item When the network condition deteriorates, the video resolution decreases incrementally.
\item If the user adjusts the video profile, the resolution of the video returned in the callbacks also changes.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em observer} & Video frame observer object instance. See \{\mbox{\hyperlink{interfaceio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1video_1_1_i_video_frame_observer}{I\+Video\+Frame\+Observer\}. 0\+: Success.$<$ 0\+: Failure. }}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{setCloudProxy@{setCloudProxy}!io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine@{io.agora.rtc2.RtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setCloudProxy()}{setCloudProxy()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+set\+Cloud\+Proxy (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{proxy\+Type }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Sets the Agora cloud proxy service.

When the user\textquotesingle{}s firewall restricts the IP address and port, refer to {\itshape Use Cloud Proxy} to add the specific IP addresses and ports to the firewall whitelist; then, call this method to enable the cloud proxy and set the {\ttfamily proxy\+Type} parameter as {\ttfamily T\+R\+A\+N\+S\+P\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+D\+P\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+X\+Y(1)}, which is the cloud proxy for the U\+DP protocol.

After a successfully cloud proxy connection, the S\+DK triggers the \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_acf3ab9feae0d9a6001da31e95363aa22}{on\+Connection\+State\+Changed\}{\ttfamily (C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+NG, C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+C\+H\+A\+N\+G\+E\+D\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+T\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+X\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+E\+R\+V\+ER)} callback. To disable the cloud proxy that has been set, call {\ttfamily set\+Cloud\+Proxy(\+N\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+X\+Y)}. To change the cloud proxy type that has been set, call {\ttfamily set\+Cloud\+Proxy(\+N\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+X\+Y)} first, and then call {\ttfamily set\+Cloud\+Proxy}, and pass the value that you expect in {\ttfamily proxy\+Type}. Agora recommends that you call this method before joining the channel or after leaving the channel.For the S\+DK v3.\+3.\+x, the services for pushing streams to C\+DN and co-\/hosting across channels are not available when you use the cloud proxy for the U\+DP protocol. For the S\+DK v3.\+4.\+0 and later, the services for pushing streams to C\+DN and co-\/hosting across channels are not available when the user is in a network environment with a firewall and uses the cloud proxy for the U\+DP protocol.  proxy\+Type The cloud proxy type. This parameter is required, and the S\+DK reports an error if you do not pass in a value. The cloud proxy types include\+: Constants\#\+T\+R\+A\+N\+S\+P\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+XY T\+R\+A\+N\+S\+P\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+X\+Y(0)\} Constants\#\+T\+R\+A\+N\+S\+P\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+D\+P\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+XY T\+R\+A\+N\+S\+P\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+D\+P\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+X\+Y(1)\} 0\+: Success.$<$ 0\+: Failure.{\ttfamily -\/2(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+R\+G\+U\+M\+E\+NT)}\+: The parameter is invalid.{\ttfamily -\/7(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+I\+N\+I\+T\+I\+A\+L\+I\+Z\+ED)}\+: The S\+DK is not initialized. }}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a39207f6b1f7136fe8faf6ef15915b97d}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a39207f6b1f7136fe8faf6ef15915b97d}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enableWirelessAccelerate()}{enableWirelessAccelerate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily abstract int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Rtc\+Engine.\+enable\+Wireless\+Accelerate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{boolean}]{enabled }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [abstract]}}

Turn W\+I\+FI acceleration on or off.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This method is called before and after joining a channel.
\item Users check the W\+I\+FI router app for information about acceleration. Therefore, if this interface is invoked, the caller accepts that the caller\textquotesingle{}s name will be displayed to the user in the W\+I\+FI router application on behalf of the caller.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em enabled} & 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+Turn W\+I\+FI acceleration on.
\item false\+Turn W\+I\+FI acceleration off.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
